commit d90907784a4f422acce9cc6937e58c3db2076285
Author: AlexeyBarabash <alexey@brave.com>
Date:   Mon Jun 1 18:06:41 2026 +0300

    amend! [cr150][Android] WIP OmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter refactored
    
    [cr150][Android] OmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter refactored
    
    Upstream moved view type registration, inflation, and binding logic out
    of OmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter into a new OmniboxViewHolderFactory.
    Brave previously registered BRAVE_SEARCH_PROMO_BANNER and
    BRAVE_LEO_SUGGESTION types in BraveOmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter's
    constructor. With the refactor, those types must now be registered in the
    factory instead.
    
    Fix: introduce BraveOmniboxViewHolderFactory (extends
    OmniboxViewHolderFactory) that registers Brave types in its constructor,
    and redirect new OmniboxViewHolderFactory() to
    new BraveOmniboxViewHolderFactory() via bytecode. Since registerType() is
    private in OmniboxViewHolderFactory, the DummySuper + changeMethodOwner
    pattern (same as BraveIntentHandlerInternal) is used to expose it at
    compile time. BraveOmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter and its bytecode
    adapter are removed as they are no longer needed.
    
    Verified:
    - BRAVE_LEO_SUGGESTION: tap omnibox and type — Leo suggestion appears.
    - BRAVE_SEARCH_PROMO_BANNER: launch with
      --enable-features=BraveSearchOmniboxBanner, set non-Brave DSE, clear
      promo prefs, set locale to US/GB/DE/FR/CA/AT/ES/MX, type in omnibox —
      banner appears.
    
    Chromium change:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/ccc8042b3f78b7b8aa1c7b8be253d324420bc2cc
    
    commit ccc8042b3f78b7b8aa1c7b8be253d324420bc2cc
    Author: Peter Kang <peterkang@google.com>
    Date:   Wed May 27 13:47:54 2026 -0700
    
        Implemented async view inflation through background thread

        OmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter into a new OmniboxViewHolderFactory.

commit 4b26c22c9b94cc2028ffd1849b95212f6db30611
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Sun May 31 08:53:26 2026 +0100

    [cr150][toolchain] Update the Rust/WASM toolchain
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/c8f90bb14a9aa298d43bb310d2ef7890d5562b8f
    
    commit c8f90bb14a9aa298d43bb310d2ef7890d5562b8f
    Author: Lukasz Anforowicz <lukasza@chromium.org>
    Date:   Tue May 19 09:59:57 2026 -0700
    
        [crubit] Roll to ToT + build w/ `--locked` + install `*.gn` files.
    
        This CL re-packages Crubit for distribution under
        `third_party/rust-toolchain`:
    
        * Crubit has been rolled to ToT (as of 2026-05-18).  This includes:
            - Adding `Cargo.lock` (bf286595f226508de5c3baaf61c8b2a573a31022)
            - Tweaks to `BUILD.gn` files (7ef002fc07dbdf217fa984f31122896e03e63)
            - `Iterator::next` fix (a123430d0bf3363db79a742948e2b3a552c428f7)
        * `build_crubit.py` has been updated to:
            - Pass `--locked` when running `cargo build`.  This ensures
              deterministic builds that are more resilient to supply chain attacks
              as tracked by https://crbug.com/510364826
            - Install / copy additional files to
              `third_party/rust-toolchain/lib/cribit`: `BUILD.gn` and
              `crubit.gni`.  These files are needed for avoiding manual
              replication of Crubit-side build rules into Chromium as tracked in
              https://crbug.com/507146475
    
        A side-effect of this CL is that it verifies and confirms that
        https://crrev.com/c/7808305 works as intended - it allows using
        `rustversion` in a way that succeeds building a bleeding edge Crubit
        with a slightly older `rustc` (the one that is currently packaged and
        used in Chromium).
    
        Fixed: 510364826
        Bug: 507146475
        Change-Id: Id7c737d8f117fc9d4d72d25f5b80d29c40702ade
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7831417
        Commit-Queue: Łukasz Anforowicz <lukasza@chromium.org>

    [brockit] Add `update-rust-wasm-toolchain` command
    
    This PR adds a command to `brockit` to be used to update the Rust/WASM
    toolchain. This command will take care of determining which version we
    should be using, and going ahead and fetching whatever is available in
    the bucket, based on the available indexes.
    
    Bug: https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/55812

commit c532caf7ec723085fab5916c348da0ad6d350f50
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Sun May 31 05:02:38 2026 +0100

    [brockit] Kick out Rust/WASM CI jobs
    
    This PR adds a new command to brockit, `brockit
    gen-rust-wasm-toolchain`, which will be used to kick out a new toolchain
    run across all platforms.
    
    This is the first use of CI in `brockit`, but we potentially want this
    type of thing for all toolchains, so further work will follow to make
    this code more generic to other CI tasks.
    
    This is a very experimental implementation.
    
    Bug: https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/55812

commit a95727ef912352aac26b85cf7c45eac71e75c86b
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Sun May 31 06:58:54 2026 +0100

    [cr150] `FollowRedirect` bundling all args into one struct
    
    This function now passes around `HttpRequestHeadersUpdateParams`.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/d210a4a1f5f1937af4eb312e9b2d8cc7f9306b0f
    
    commit d210a4a1f5f1937af4eb312e9b2d8cc7f9306b0f
    Author: Hiroshige Hayashizaki <hiroshige@chromium.org>
    Date:   Fri May 29 15:58:53 2026 -0700
    
        Use HttpRequestHeadersUpdateParams in mojom::URLLoader::FollowRedirect
    
        Follow-up of https://crrev.com/c/7835601 that introduced
        `network::HttpRequestHeadersUpdateParams`.
    
        This CL uses `network.mojom.HttpRequestHeadersUpdateParams` (defined
        in https://crrev.com/c/7869458) in
        `network::mojom::URLLoader::FollowRedirect` in
        `services/network/public/mojom/url_loader.mojom`, and adjust its
        overrides accordingly.
    
        ### Purely mechanical changes (See Patch Set 35):
    
        Replaces
        ```
        FollowRedirect\(\s*
        const std::vector<std::string>&\s*\w*,\s*
        const (::)?net::HttpRequestHeaders&\s*\w*,\s*
        const (::)?net::HttpRequestHeaders&\s*\w*,
        ```
          with
        ```
        FollowRedirect(
            network::HttpRequestHeadersUpdateParams headers_update_params,
        ```
    
        Replaces the followings (ignoring whitespaces):
        ```
        FollowRedirect({}, {}, {}, std::nullopt)
        FollowRedirect({}, {}, {}, {})
        FollowRedirect(/*removed_headers=*/{},
                       /*modified_headers=*/{},
                       /*modified_cors_exempt_headers=*/{},
                       /*new_url=*/std::nullopt)
        FollowRedirect(/*removed_headers=*/{},
                       /*modified_headers=*/{},
                       /*modified_cors_exempt_headers=*/{},
                       std::nullopt)
        FollowRedirect(
            std::vector<std::string>() /* sremoved_headers */,
            net::HttpRequestHeaders() /* modified_headers */,
            net::HttpRequestHeaders() /* smodified_cors_exempt_headers*/,
            std::nullopt)
        ```
    
        with
    
        ```
        FollowRedirect(/*headers_update_params=*/{}, /*new_url=*/std::nullopt)
        ```
    
        ### Manual changes
    
        Still mostly straightforward, with notable manual changes:
    
        - `PrefetchURLLoader` has been intentionally dropped some of
          `HttpRequestHeadersUpdateParams` since before. This CL has
          additional lines to preserve the existing behavior:
          - `content/browser/loader/prefetch_url_loader.cc`
        - Before this CL, we had some copies just because `FollowRedirect()`
          has been passing `const&` arguments. This CL removes the copies and
          modifies the passed `headers_update_params` directly.
          - `android_webview/browser/network_service/aw_proxying_url_loader_factory.cc`
          - `chrome/browser/signin/chrome_signin_proxying_url_loader_factory.cc`
          - `content/browser/loader/subresource_proxying_url_loader.cc`
          - `services/network/cors/cors_url_loader.cc`
    
        Bug: 511306597, 434292502
        Change-Id: Ib3c70b9f986a543bdf93e7a97a9212a8a756a600

commit 98876b97b180df134f5b9af5964b2df0542baf24
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Sun May 31 06:53:33 2026 +0100

    [cr150] `os_crypt_async::Encryptor` now refcounted
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/10801327968664eebe6e1ef2eafb5b271bc61a7b
    
    commit 10801327968664eebe6e1ef2eafb5b271bc61a7b
    Author: Jeffrey Gour <jeffreygour@microsoft.com>
    Date:   Fri May 29 09:05:28 2026 -0700
    
        Make os_crypt_async::Encryptor ref counted
    
        This CL updates the os_crypt_async::Encryptor to be ref counted so that
        it can be shared by multiple owners using scoped_refptr.
    
        Since ref counted objects must be managed by scoped_refptr and are not
        copyable or moveable all current consumers had to be updated for this
        change. Thus this CL touches a large number of files, but the vast
        majority of the changes are simply change Encryptor instances to
        scoped_refptr<Encryptor>.
    
        One change that is not immediately obvious is the change needed to
        encryptor_mojom_traits. Since the cpp type is now a nullable
        scoped_refptr rather than a raw object, the trait typemap needed to be
        update to set nullable_is_same_type to true. This in turn requires that
        the StructTraits object implement IsNull and SetToNull. So these methods
        were added. A new test block was added to

    This plaster was a bit naive on its matching. This change make the
    plaster match the class delcaration and insert at the end.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/2a7b549b8a7bee0ffbb6cca4a9f0d11b9d7c617c
    
    commit 2a7b549b8a7bee0ffbb6cca4a9f0d11b9d7c617c
    Author: Deepak Ravichandran <deepakr@google.com>
    Date:   Fri May 29 08:18:41 2026 -0700
    
        Refactor startup URL validation to block navigation laundering
    
        This refactors startup URL validation by introducing separate
        ValidateLaunchUrlWebSafe and ValidateLaunchUrlWebUnsafe contexts. The
        custom google-chrome:// scheme protocol handler is strictly restricted
        to only route WebSafe inner URLs, and all nested filesystem: and blob:
        schemes are blocked for it to prevent privileged origin laundering from
        both in-browser and cross-browser launch vectors.
    
        Note that these changes only affect the disabled-by-default
        kGoogleChromeScheme feature flag, and thus this CL does not affect
        default browser behavior yet (except for the nested scheme blocks).
    
        Additionally, this uses an opaque origin as the initiator in any
        google-chrome:// scheme cases that lack an initiator (both at the
        browser-side protocol handler and the startup command-line parser), as a
        way to further limit the navigation's privileges and enforce a secure
        fallback behavior.
    
        Bug: 513728023, 490448948, b:446672134
        Change-Id: I873a4cf8f50429f91ff253e2b02cb28e303544ff
        Tests: UrlUtilTest.*
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7870110

commit 67c94005b7fa06e28de1a778459c4975cc83b836
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 29 12:24:46 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Pin Dawn's Go toolchain to `1.26.1` via `dawn_go_version`
    
    Dawn's Tint codegen step (`run.py gen sources`) runs a Go program whose `go.mod`
    now requires Go >= 1.25.0, but Dawn still pins its provisioned Go
    toolchain (`dawn_go_version`) at 1.21.3. On most machines this is masked by Go's
    automatic toolchain switching (GOTOOLCHAIN=auto), which downloads a newer Go on
    demand. Our builds shouldn't depend on a build-time Go download, so when that
    switch doesn't happen the build fails with:
    
          go: go.mod requires go >= 1.25.0 (running go 1.21.3)
    
    Override dawn_go_version via the Chromium solution's custom_vars so the
    provisioned bootstrap Go already satisfies go.mod. This is applied at gclient
    sync time (before the CIPD package is fetched), unlike a patch to Dawn's DEPS
    which would land after sync. 1.26.1 is the same infra/3pp/tools/go version
    already pinned elsewhere in-tree (BoringSSL), so it's known-good and
    known-available.
    
    No code or build-output behavior changes; this only selects a newer Go to run an
    existing codegen step.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/_/dawn/dawn/+/4634a32c28f9f0d57f1c04f9fda0bff35c0787f0
    
    commit 4634a32c28f9f0d57f1c04f9fda0bff35c0787f0
    Author: Kai Ninomiya <kainino@chromium.org>
    Date:   Wed Apr 29 08:08:00 2026 -0700
    
        [infra] Update dependency on go.chromium.org/luci
    
        This is an updated copy of
        https://dawn-review.git.corp.google.com/c/dawn/+/304855 originally
        authored by kainino@.
    
        - go get go.chromium.org/luci@latest
        - go mod tidy
        - Get Gemini to help fix the errors
          - API changes
          - fstestoswrapper updated to maintain identical behavior to the
            real filesystem after several test-only symlink behavior changes
            in Go 1.25
    
        Note this does NOT update other dependencies.
    
        Fixes: 505830926
        Change-Id: I1ed4e5a728ea040fada22d958bf37c2de0787f69

    [cr150][needs-plaster] Add `legacy_wrapper` dep to DevTools network module
    
    `RequestAdblockView.ts` imports `legacy_wrapper`, but the network
    `devtools_ui_module` no longer declares it as a dependency, so a clean build

    Author: Elly <ellyjones@chromium.org>
    Date:   Thu May 28 13:08:15 2026 -0700
    
        net: remove deprecated HashValue constructors
    
        After this change, net::HashValue only has one constructor: the
        two-argument (tag, span) variant. The tag is const; the fingerprint
        can't be const because it needs to be written inside the constructor,
        but there's no externally exposed way to write it. The overall type is
        now an immutable value type.
    
        This requires one slightly awkward hack in one of the SCT unit tests:
        since HashValue is const now, it has no assignment operator, which
        forces a bit of code restructuring.

commit 6b0f6f5d530795b1d0e1705fba8f9359cbf6861d
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 29 12:50:47 2026 +0100

    [cr150][needs-plaster] `ExtensionsMenuHandler::OnExtensionToggleSelected` changed
    
    This function now expects an origin to be passed in.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/e6f8ab61283e2eca8ee75188cfb0421215215292
    
    commit e6f8ab61283e2eca8ee75188cfb0421215215292
    Author: Eva Su <evasu@chromium.org>
    Date:   Thu May 28 16:58:51 2026 -0700
    
        [Extensions] Fix TOCTOU vulnerability in site access toggle
    
        This CL fixes a Time-of-Check Time-of-Use (TOCTOU) vulnerability in the
        extensions menu site access toggle, and implements the suggested fix by
        binding the site-access action to the origin that was active when the
        user initiated the click.
    
        Previously, the target origin for permission changes was resolved from
        the active WebContents at the moment of the click. Because the menu
        remains open during page navigations, an attacker could initiate a
        navigation to a sensitive site right before the click was processed,
        leading to the extension being granted access to the new, sensitive
        origin instead of the original one.
    
        We also add checks for IsRestrictedUrl to prevent potential race
        conditions where the UI to allow changing permission settings for a site
        even if the extension is fundamentally barred from running there. These
        checks ensure that permission changes are only considered for valid,
        non-restricted origins and that the UI state correctly reflects that
        permissions cannot be granted or altered on these sensitive sites.
    
        For full consistency, we should also update AllowHostAccessRequest() to
        use the target_origin, however, this is lower priority since it’s
        typically triggered by a more immediate UI action, but I’ll handle this
        separately in a follow-up CL (crrev.com/c/7865583) since this one is
        already getting quite large.
    
        Fixed: 513553557
        Change-Id: I7bb8dbe11665cef4a1076fd748d256683a9035f8
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7853880
        Commit-Queue: Eva Su <evasu@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Tim <tjudkins@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1638068}

commit 40605c834a0867112af266ccc05464e150d9e11c

commit 757332044680ab3c55bdef819cef6cb4ea1f5853
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 16:01:10 2026 -0400

    [cr150][WIP] Fix GN "Assignment had no effect" error in apple toolchain on non-mac hosts
    
    Upstream's `single_apple_toolchain` reads `_toolchain_args` only inside the
    `use_apple_linker && expression`, whose leading `host_os == "mac"` term
    short-circuits on non-mac hosts (e.g. cross-compiling mac from Linux), leaving
    the alias assigned-but-unused and tripping GN's hard error. Mark it with
    `not_needed()` to keep the variable in use regardless of host.
    
    We're going to upstream this change.
    
    The error message was:
    
    + npm run build -- Component -C mac_Component --channel=nightly --target_os=mac --target_arch=x64 --target=brave:all --gn=symbol_level:0
    generate ninja files
      ERROR at //build/toolchain/apple/toolchain.gni:109:23: Assignment had no effect.
          _toolchain_args = invoker.toolchain_args
                            ^---------------------
      You set the variable "_toolchain_args" here and it was unused before it went
      out of scope.
    
      Via these template invocations:
        mac_toolchain("clang_arm64")  //build/toolchain/mac/BUILD.gn:56
        apple_toolchain("clang_arm64")  //build/toolchain/mac/BUILD.gn:16
        single_apple_toolchain("clang_arm64")  //build/toolchain/apple/toolchain.gni:1008
    
      See //build/toolchain/apple/toolchain.gni:1008:3: whence it was called.
        single_apple_toolchain(target_name) {
        ^------------------------------------
      See //build/toolchain/mac/BUILD.gn:16:3: whence it was called.
        apple_toolchain(target_name) {
        ^-----------------------------
      See //build/toolchain/mac/BUILD.gn:56:1: whence it was called.
      mac_toolchain("clang_arm64") {
      ^-----------------------------
      See //BUILD.gn:87:1: which caused the file to be included.
      group("gn_all") {
      ^----------------
      null
    Process exited with code 1
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/7842f920ed859ef5b7928e2d5d9915c5cc8d0a4a
    
    commit 7842f920ed859ef5b7928e2d5d9915c5cc8d0a4a
    Author: Ryosuke Miyake <rysk@google.com>
    Date:   Tue May 26 04:59:23 2026 -0700
    
        Reland "Roll out Apple Linker for macOS non-official builds"
    
        This is a reland of commit a086c9b72ef72d618f563cc17847d77011a8e6d8. The
        original CL was reverted in crrev.com/c/7835271 because it broke the x64
        debug build on the arm64 Mac bot `mac-updater-builder-dbg`:
        https://ci.chromium.org/ui/p/chromium/builders/ci/mac-updater-builder-dbg/270431/infra
    
        Reason for Revert & Fix: The original rollout crashed with `Segmentation
        fault: 11` in `clang++` during the link step of `UpdaterSetup` on the
        `mac-updater-builder-dbg` bot (an arm64 host cross-compiling a x64
        target).
    
        To bypass this toolchain crash safely, this CL restricts the default
        `use_apple_linker` to native macOS builds only (`current_cpu ==
        host_cpu`). Cross-compilation builds on CI bots will automatically fall
        back to LLD, which has been fully verified to compile and link
        successfully.
    
        Additionally, we resolved secondary toolchain compile failures observed
        on cross-compiling trybots (e.g., `mac_chromium_compile_rel_ng` missing
        `-B` and `-fuse-ld=lld` flags for host tools like `nasm`). We fixed this
        by generalizing `use_apple_linker` and `use_lld` re-evaluations inside
        `single_apple_toolchain`'s `toolchain_args` to perfectly align GN's
        parent (toolchain definition) and child (target compilation) contexts.
    
        Gerrit IFTTT comments have also been added to guarantee long-term
        synchronization between the global declared arguments and toolchain
        re-evaluations.
    
        Original change's description:
        > Switches the default linker on macOS to the Apple linker
        > (ld64/ld-prime) for non-official (developer and bot) builds to speed up
        > iteration time.
        >
        > LLD continues to be used for official builds (is_official_build=true)
        > and when ThinLTO is enabled, to maintain production performance
        > characteristics. ThinLTO is now explicitly tied to LLD support.
        >
        > Benchmark Results (MacBook Pro, M4 Max):
        > - Component Debug (libchrome_dll):
        >   - Cold Cache: 4.38x speedup (5.6s vs 24.7s)
        >   - Hot Cache: 3.39x speedup (3.6s vs 12.2s)
        > - Component Release (libchrome_dll):
        >   - Cold Cache: 3.72x speedup (2.5s vs 9.2s)
        >   - Hot Cache: 2.43x speedup (1.7s vs 4.1s)
        > - Non-Component (Chromium Framework):
        >   - Cold Cache: 6.81x speedup (6.4s vs 43.8s)
        >   - Hot Cache: 3.83x speedup (4.4s vs 16.9s)
    
        Based on original work in crrev.com/c/7784858.
    
        Bug: 502338406
        Change-Id: I707321eeac39043922571c2425a4a52fdc1ea7ca
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7839163
        Mega-CQ: Ryosuke Miyake <rysk@google.com>
        Reviewed-by: Takuto Ikuta <tikuta@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Junji Watanabe <jwata@google.com>
        Commit-Queue: Ryosuke Miyake <rysk@google.com>
        Auto-Submit: Ryosuke Miyake <rysk@google.com>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1636081}

commit e386c7f71fa9ceddded64bcdfe861d7726c4d454
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 15:04:46 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Fix MV2 exception list to use hashed extension IDs
    
    `BuildBraveMV2ExceptionList` was pushing raw extension IDs into a list that the
    upstream impact checker compares against `HashedExtensionId` values, so the
    exemption never matched and the four supported MV2 extensions got disabled on
    restart once the stage-relaxing override was removed. Move the helper from
    `constants_impl` (which can't link `HashedExtensionId`) into the impact-checker
    override and hash the IDs before joining.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/e768ae9db49404408d13d22a4e9f7d81b095dab8
    
    commit e768ae9db49404408d13d22a4e9f7d81b095dab8
    Author: Devlin Cronin <rdevlin.cronin@chromium.org>
    Date:   Fri May 22 16:01:04 2026 -0700
    
        [Extensions] Remove kExtensionManifestV2Disabled feature
    
        The kExtensionManifestV2Disabled feature has been default-enabled for
        over a year. Remove the feature and the effectively-dead code.
    
        Any tests that relied on being in the "warning" phase (i.e., with the
        kExtensionManifestV2Disabled) for their sole behavior testing are
        removed, since this stage is no longer reachable.
    
        This CL should have no behavior change in production.
    
        Bug: 431097630

commit a11fca35161aef25a72c98918a492fa9199fb538
Author: AlexeyBarabash <alexey@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 13:48:33 2026 +0300

    [cr150][Android] WIP OmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter refactored
    
    New arg at ctor - OmniboxViewHolderFactory
    Types registration is moved to OmniboxViewHolderFactory.ctor
    
    Chromium change:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/ccc8042b3f78b7b8aa1c7b8be253d324420bc2cc
    
    commit ccc8042b3f78b7b8aa1c7b8be253d324420bc2cc
    Author: Peter Kang <peterkang@google.com>
    Date:   Wed May 27 13:47:54 2026 -0700
    
        Implemented async view inflation through background thread
    
        Fix Omnibox asynchronous view inflation architecture
    
        Resolve a silent failure in the view pre-warming flow that occurs when
        Omnibox asynchronous view inflation is enabled. This failure stems from
        a lifecycle disconnect where view pre-creation aborts due to a missing
        UI data adapter reference.
    
        Extract view type registration, inflation, and binding logic out of
        OmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter into a new OmniboxViewHolderFactory.
        This decouples view generation from backing data, allowing the
        background thread to safely instantiate the view factory alongside the
        PreWarmingRecycledViewPool. The data-dependent adapter is now
        constructed and applied on the UI thread only after layout inflation
        completes. Additionally, initiate view pre-warming directly at the end
        of the dropdown's construction lifecycle to bypass the bypassed
        coordinator-to-pool initialization signal.
    
        Change-Id: If23a7c942ae8333c7d8f3b8b11bc693d2bbe68d6
        Bug: 514728907
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7852959
        Commit-Queue: Peter Kang <peterkang@google.com>
        Reviewed-by: Patrick Noland <pnoland@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Sky Malice <skym@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1637203}

    macros are used.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/9faab1a9bfbfbd26e79408965ff938ed2a464cb2
    
    commit 9faab1a9bfbfbd26e79408965ff938ed2a464cb2
    Author: Judith Hemp <hempjudith@google.com>
    Date:   Wed May 27 11:24:52 2026 -0700
    
        [clapper] Persist "Subscribe" button in Page Info
    
        This CL makes the Notifications page info entry with the Subscribe
        button persist for the whole lifetime of the document after the page
        has requested notification permission. In order to simplify the UI,
        the Subscribe button is also displayed if the permission is embargoed.
    
        This functionality is gated behind a new feature flag, disabled by
        default, and is meant to be activated together with ClapperLoud, with
        the goal to ensure that the Subscribe button can always be used in Page
        Info after the page requested notification permission.

commit ef1f9b31710155f2cd203e5876bac51d91606f3c
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 06:13:35 2026 +0100

    [cr150] `ResolveProxy` test call fixed
    
    This function now needs a `NetworkHandle` by the caller.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/a1e22b511ad067e2631aca13d5ad73d27bb4778d
    
    commit a1e22b511ad067e2631aca13d5ad73d27bb4778d
    Author: Stefano Duo <stefanoduo@google.com>
    Date:   Wed May 27 04:56:56 2026 -0700
    
        Support target_network in proxy resolution logic
    
        This is necessary to support true multinetworking in Chromium.
    
        The implementation follows a top-down approach: we start from //net's
        entry points, then slowly flow towards the low-level primitives that
        require the target network.
    
        The opposite approach would be to start accepting a target_network in
        low-level primitives, then slowly start bubbling it up. This other
        approach would require sprinkling the codebase with
        handles::kInvalidNetworkHandle, which would then be later on be cleaned
        up as the bubbling up happens, making it more likely to forget to update
        a call site in the process.
    
        Bug: 495684670
        Change-Id: If341a59d1bb1f65274d26531c36f2588f0d0873b
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7612171
        Commit-Queue: Stefano Duo <stefanoduo@google.com>
        Reviewed-by: Adam Rice <ricea@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1636857}

              ^---------------------------------------------------------
    It is not in any dependency of
      //brave/browser/ui:ui
    The include file is in the target(s):

    which should somehow be reachable.
    
    Chromium change:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/cef22632e31017d245887a528a69fad57884f009
    
    commit cef22632e31017d245887a528a69fad57884f009
    Author: Erik Chen <erikchen@chromium.org>
    Date:   Tue May 26 08:50:09 2026 -0700
    
        Modularize: move android/ sources from //chrome/browser:browser to //chrome/browser/android
    
        Extract 326 production source files in chrome/browser/android/ from
        the static_library("browser") if(is_android) block into a new
        source_set("android") in //chrome/browser/android, along with the
        corresponding deps and allow_circular_includes_from entries.
    
        The 10 top-level *_android.cc/h files (after_startup_task_utils_android,
        browser_process_platform_part_android, chrome_browser_main_android,
        chrome_content_browser_client_android, icon_loader_android,
        memory_details_android, platform_util_android, shell_integration_android,
        chrome_browser_interface_binders_webui_parts_android) remain in
        //chrome/browser:browser, as does the small set under commerce/android,
        composeplate/android, incognito/android, prefetch/android, and
        preloading/android. Those will move in follow-up CLs as their respective
        subdirectories are componentized.
    
        Three small if(is_android) deps blocks at the //chrome/browser:browser
        level (paint_preview, guest_view, and the enable_vr VR blocks) move
        into //chrome/browser/android's deps with their outer feature conditions
        preserved.
    
        A handful of test/wrapper targets pick up a direct dep on
        //chrome/browser/android because they used to reach those headers via
        the monolith. Three sibling targets get //chrome/browser/android added
        to their visibility lists. Two consumer .cc files in
        //chrome/browser/offline_pages/android and one in
        //chrome/browser/printing pick up // nogncheck on a header include that
        moved out of the monolith and would otherwise require an :impl-target
        dep on //chrome/browser/android that creates a GN dependency cycle.
    
        gn check passes on out/linux, out/mac, out/win, out/chromeos,
        out/android, and out/android-cast-arm-rel.
    
        Bug: 353332589
        Change-Id: Id80fd22aaedabb514f60bdc312a171cf85e1f57a
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7874571

commit 6ce4b3f98c069461ed94df305b6be4e74c380521
Author: AlexeyBarabash <alexey@brave.com>
Date:   Wed May 27 22:46:18 2026 +0300

    [cr150][Android] Fixed gn_check error at form_data_parser.h
    
    Message:
    
    ERROR at //brave/browser/password_manager/android/password_ui_view_android.cc:39:11: Can't include this header from here.
              ^-----------------------------------------------------------------------
    The target:
      //chrome/browser:browser
    is including a file from the target:
      //components/password_manager/core/browser/form_parsing:form_parsing
    
    It's usually best to depend directly on the destination target.
    In some cases, the destination target is considered a subcomponent
    of an intermediate target. In this case, the intermediate target
    should depend publicly on the destination to forward the ability
    to include headers.
    
    Dependency chain (there may also be others):
      //chrome/browser:browser -->
      //chrome/browser/password_manager:impl --[private]-->
      //components/password_manager/core/browser/form_parsing:form_parsing

commit f52ae87261d23990d324ab9a2b4e99f90b5668d1
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Wed May 27 14:13:06 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Clone print-preview settings for new `GetPrintPreviewParams()` IPC
    
    Upstream's `PrintPreview` IPC no longer carries settings back to the browser;
    the renderer fetches them via `PrintManagerHost.GetPrintPreviewParams()`, which
    pops from `PrintViewManagerBase`'s queue. Enqueue here so the renderer's
    subsequent fetch succeeds.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/ea38e74cf233e5ae1e5c3cc7d02d3c36e025a754
    
    commit ea38e74cf233e5ae1e5c3cc7d02d3c36e025a754
    Author: Lei Zhang <thestig@chromium.org>
    Date:   Fri May 22 14:26:51 2026 -0700
    
        Print Preview: Remove PrintManagerHost.UpdatePrintSettings() dict param
    
        In the Print Preview IPC dance, PrintPreviewHandler in the browser calls
        PrintRenderFrame.PrintPreview() with a print settings dictionary.
        PrintRenderFrameHelper, the PrintRenderFrame implementation,
        conditionally makes a small edit to the dictionary, and passes it back
        to PrintViewManagerBase in the browser in the
        PrintManagerHost.UpdatePrintSettings() call.
    
        In modern Chromium, the browser process can make the same conditional
        decision and modify the dictionary itself. As such, there is no need for
        PrintRenderFrameHelper to pass it back. So simplify the
        UpdatePrintSettings() Mojo interface to remove the dictionary parameter.
        After this, rename it to GetPrintPreviewParams() since it is no longer
        sending an update to the browser.
    
        On the browser side, pass the dictionary from PrintPreviewHandler to
        PrintViewManagerBase, to compensate for the IPC change. The dictionary
        needs to go into a queue as there may be multiple
        PrintRenderFrame.PrintPreview() calls in quick succession.
    
        Update tests as needed to match the IPC changes. In several test cases,
        calls TestPrintViewManager::CreateForWebContents() to properly install
        the TestPrintViewManager, instead of allocating it on the stack.
    
        Bug: 513005991
        Change-Id: Ie022900568c3bac7e086c9fbf9d6345a22e46278
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7866423
        Reviewed-by: Andy Phan <andyphan@chromium.org>
        Commit-Queue: Lei Zhang <thestig@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Tom Sepez <tsepez@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1635224}

commit 236eba2ff9e9a7e2c8d90aa3f4c5846e1af46ec5
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Wed May 27 12:40:10 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Skip orphan containers in browsing data delegate
    
    `BraveBrowsingDataRemoverDelegate::RemoveEmbedderData` previously iterated every
    locally-used container — orphans included — and issued a `RemoveWithFilter` per
    partition, which instantiated the partition:(`can_create=true`): and let its
    storage backends recreate the on-disk directory that
    `ContainersService::ScheduleOrphanedContainersCleanup` was trying to delete.
    Filter to synced containers only; orphans are wiped wholesale by the orphan
    cleanup path.
    
    Fixes `ContainersBrowserTest.RemovedContainerCleanupAfterRestore`, which was
    failing like this:

commit b8affaa8cf5fe5c9cf30f925791e5917569fadc5
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Wed May 27 10:58:08 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Only preserve `kPrefProvider` rules in `ContentSettingsDefaultsKeeper`
    
    The keeper snapshotted every wildcard shields rule whose source wasn't
    `kDefaultProvider`, then re-applied them through the user pref store --
    including policy-provided defaults (e.g. AdBlockOnlyMode's `BRAVE_REFERRERS =
    ALLOW`), which would survive as user-level rules after the policy was removed.
    Restrict the filter to `kPrefProvider` so only user-owned rules are preserved;
    other providers re-publish their own state.
    
    This fixes `AdblockOnlyModeBrowserTest.AdblockOnlyModeDisablingRestoresSettings`
    which was failing like this:

    commit c2cdba108e94519b5fd306a086590de3ab34a902
    Author: James Cook <jamescook@chromium.org>
    Date:   Tue May 26 15:49:38 2026 -0700
    
        extensions: Add chrome/common/extensions unit tests to desktop Android
    
        These tests were missed during desktop Android bring-up. They mostly
        pass without modification. A few exceptions:
    
        * Some used APIs that are not supported by Android as test data (e.g.
          bookmarkManagerPrivate is not supported because the bookmarks page
          on Android is native UI). I switched these to APIs that are supported
          on all platform (e.g. runtime).
        * One file tested browserAction, which is not supported in MV3. I
          skipped it and added a static_assert !IS_ANDROID.
    
        I also moved the unit test file references from chrome/test/BUILD.gn
        to chrome/common/extensions/BUILD.gn to be closer to the actual files.
    
        Finally I deleted a stale TODO about Windows support -- the comment it
        refers to doesn't exist anymore.

commit cbc22b7339d07f8c91f36a5b645faeac7e0ba210
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Wed May 27 10:27:13 2026 +0100

    [plaster][cr150] `BrowserViewTabbedLayoutImpl` overrides rework
    
    This class has undergone a good amount of changes. It has dropped a lot
    of members, like `TopSeparatorType`, `ShadowOverlayVisible`, etc, and it
    has moved all these calculation into `DoPreLayoutComputations`.
    
    This change reconciles our own pre-exsiting override with this new class
    layout. `CalculateSeparatorInfo()` has been introduced, and
    `suppress_top_separator` is now dropped as a function arugment. In
    particular, our definition of
    `BraveBrowserViewTabbedLayoutImpl::CalculateSeparatorInfo` is left in
    the shadow file, to allow us to see the definition of `SeparatorInfo`,
    which has been moved out of the public interface, and has required some
    very labourious plumbing of values for tests.
    
    Plaster have been introduced to reduce the need of `#define` macros.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/7635cb9367ddbeebfb8902b07bcd51eae7f8f09b
    
    commit 7635cb9367ddbeebfb8902b07bcd51eae7f8f09b
    Author: Dana Fried <dfried@chromium.org>
    Date:   Mon May 25 17:50:55 2026 -0700
    
        [Vertical Tabs] Simplify logic around separators and padding
    
        This simplifies the computation of horizontal layout, vertical tabs
        layout/animation, separators, and padding and ensures that these
        calculations are only done once, at the very start of layout.
    
        The values are cached and then cleared at the end of layout to prevent
        the possibility of stale values being used. The structs that hold these
        values are also moved out of the .h file and become PIMPL in order to
        reduce the complexity of the browser layout's public API.
    
        After this CL, it will be explicit whether, for example, there is a top
        separator, what the "neutral" state of the VTS top corner is, whether
        contents are adjusted during side panel animations for a hidden
        separator, etc. and furthermore where these choices should be made in
        case they need to be modified in the future.
    
        Bug: 513263977
        Change-Id: I6bd110aa70fb644c341ecd3ecb4052fd9a7720ad
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7818262
        Reviewed-by: Eshwar Stalin <estalin@chromium.org>
        Commit-Queue: Dana Fried <dfried@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1635870}

        Using `EXPECT_CHECK_DEATH` in `TabStripModelBrowserTest`
    
        This CL replaces the use of `EXPECT_DEATH_IF_SUPPORTED` in a
        `TabStripModelBrowserTest` test with `EXPECT_CHECK_DEATH` to avoid
        failures for this test when building with `dcheck_always_on=true`, as in
        that build mode, `CHECK` messages are stripped from the binary, so this
        expactation would fail.

    commit c61de7b12be57721ea989071ccd5ce4bdf4110b2
    Author: Atharv Maan <atharvmaan@chromium.org>
    Date:   Mon May 25 11:15:45 2026 -0700
    
        DAU metric changes for Start Chrome with Windows
    
        This CL contains changes to the DAU metric (Session.TotalDuration) for
        OS launches as outlined in go/scww-metric-changes.
    
        We introduce a new histogram Session.TotalDuration.InteractiveEventStart
        that will mirror existing Session.TotalDuration except for the first
        session of an OS launch. This OS launch session will only start when an
        interactive user event is received.
    
        This enables us to test out the new OS launch DAU changes without
        affecting existing guardrail.

        [actor] TabObservationStrategy 2/4
    
        This CL consumes a TabObservationStrategy to determine whether to
        observe screenshots and DOM content after taking actions.
    
        This object is added in CL 1/4 and populated in CL 3/4.
    
        Specifically, this CL:
        - Adds feature flags kActorObserveScreenshotDefault and kActorObservePageContentDefault to control default observation behavior.
        - Plumbs TabObservationStrategy through ExecutionEngine, ActorTask, ActorKeyedService, and GlicActorTaskManager.
        - Updates TabObservationController to omit screenshot and/or page content fetching based on the strategy and feature flags, skipping observation entirely if both are omitted.
        - Adds comprehensive browsertest coverage verifying the omitting logic.

commit 1c48876cafba705077e1885720e4e427a3ca75d7
Author: AlexeyBarabash <alexey@brave.com>
Date:   Mon May 25 20:24:58 2026 +0300

    [cr150][Android] Fix background-tab animation when Brave bottom toolbar is active
    
    When isBraveBottomControlsEnabled() is true, BraveToolbarLayoutImpl hides
    R.id.tab_switcher_button (top toolbar) via maybeHideTopTabSwitcherButton().
    The upstream NewBackgroundTabAnimationData.captureState() then calls
    getGlobalVisibleRect on a GONE view, which returns an empty rect.
    setSize(0,0) is called on the fake animation button, and an assertion fires
    in getButtonLocation() on debug builds. On release builds the animation
    silently ran to the wrong destination (0,0).
    
    Fix: redirect NewBackgroundTabAnimationData constructor to
    BraveNewBackgroundTabAnimationData, which overrides
    getTabSwitcherButtonRect() — the method tabCreatedInBackground() calls to
    size and position the animation — to fall back to Brave's bottom toolbar
    tab switcher button (R.id.bottom_tab_switcher_button) when the upstream
    rect is empty and isBraveBottomControlsEnabled() is true.
    
    The override is implemented as a direct package-private method override:
    both classes share the same Java package, so no DummySuper pattern or
    makePublicMethod is needed. The bytecode adapter only needs
    redirectConstructor.
    
    Verification:
    - Default (bottom toolbar + top address bar): long-press a link →
      "Open in new tab" → link icon animates to the bottom toolbar tab
      switcher button ✓
    - Bottom toolbar + bottom address bar: same ✓
    - No bottom toolbar (e.g. split-screen small window, top-only): animation
      targets the top toolbar tab switcher button ✓
    
    Chromium change:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/bd7f626969f947257797e24122445dadd110461e
    
    commit bd7f626969f947257797e24122445dadd110461e

commit 66c3e3e3f0c7da6342969691328b5b880537248b
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Sat May 23 14:56:20 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Tolerate 1px rounding in `BraveMultiContentsViewTest` width checks
    
    `MultiContentsView::GetViewSizes` computes `std::round(0.5 * (available_size -
    resize_width))`, which hands one pane an extra pixel whenever that quantity is
    odd. The strict `width() == width()` `RunUntil` predicates could never converge
    at those widths and timed out on macOS arm64 CI. Replace the three width
    predicates with `std::abs(diff) <= 1 / > 1` so the deterministic 1px asymmetry
    is accepted while real asymmetry from `OnResize(30)` is still caught.

commit c1822944efd38cbb2f93a84f309127d7d0504a7d
Author: AlexeyBarabash <alexey@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 22 18:21:11 2026 +0300

    [cr150][Android] AutocompleteCoordinator.createViewProvider removed
    
    createViewProvider() was removed from AutocompleteCoordinator; its body
    moved into the new nested class SuggestionListViewHolderProvider. Brave
    previously intercepted this method via bytecode redirect to wrap the
    returned ViewProvider with a custom one that, when inflated, registered
    Brave-specific suggestion types via addTypes(dropdown.getAdapter()).
    
    The old inflate() wrapper waited for the upstream ViewProvider to signal
    that the view was ready (whenLoaded), then called addTypes() once the
    dropdown had an adapter attached. This was necessary because the adapter
    instance was only accessible after async inflation completed.
    
    The new approach redirects the OmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter
    constructor instead. BraveOmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter extends
    OmniboxSuggestionsDropdownAdapter and registers Brave types directly in
    its own constructor (after super(data)). This is safe because
    registerType() only stores lazy lambdas — the view factories are only
    invoked when RecyclerView requests a view via onCreateViewHolder, which
    cannot happen until after dropdown.setAdapter() is called. By that
    point the adapter already has all types registered.
    
    Verified:
    - BRAVE_LEO_SUGGESTION: tap omnibox and type — Leo suggestion appears.
    - BRAVE_SEARCH_PROMO_BANNER: launch with
      --enable-features=BraveSearchOmniboxBanner, set non-Brave DSE, clear
      promo prefs, set locale to US/GB/DE/FR/CA/AT/ES/MX, type in omnibox —
      banner appears.
    
    Chromium change:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/6cc22533ced40692769371b5d76bed3a36d72ccc
    
    commit 6cc22533ced40692769371b5d76bed3a36d72ccc

    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/2976e22e8416cf3a341294855047bb6280ced6b2
    
    commit 2976e22e8416cf3a341294855047bb6280ced6b2
    Author: Shunya Shishido <sisidovski@chromium.org>
    Date:   Thu May 21 23:55:41 2026 -0700
    
        Restrict background fetch from Service Worker context
    
        This CL introduces functionality to restrict the usage of
        `BackgroundFetchManager.fetch()` when called within a Service Worker
        global scope context. By default, invocation throws a `NotAllowedError`.
    
        Key Changes:
        - `BackgroundFetchManager.fetch()` thorws an exception if the execution
          context is service worker. This is implemented behind the killswitch.
        - Introduces the server configurable list of origins, that are allowed
          to call `fetch()` from the service worker context. This is added to
          minimize the compatibility risk.
        - Added unit tests, internal WPTs, and updated the existing browser
          tests.
    
        Change-Id: I6a267b59e67eab9e63a96f417b08af6e6fc2b6a0
        Bug: 40062121
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7867618

        Reland "Ignore category when determining whether an Intent URL is unsafe"
    
        Ignore category when determining whether an Intent URL is unsafe

commit 437d16f711046eced4be745c4bd491dd1c488a58
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 21 19:46:00 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Search source param is now added via prepopulated engines
    
    Previously, upstream added a source search query parameter via the autocomplete
    controller and we blocked it via a chromium_src override as we don't want those
    source attributions to appear in our search URLs. Upstream has now moved the
    code to the prepopulated engine for Google search only. We still don't want the
    source attribution, however, so we patch it out and migrate our tests over to
    the template url component.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/99def36fb425e4d866c8a70ec07db21c4d41d9c1
    
    commit 99def36fb425e4d866c8a70ec07db21c4d41d9c1
    Author: Nihar Majmudar <niharm@google.com>
    Date:   Fri May 15 14:02:57 2026 -0700
    
        [omnibox] Add source param through prepopulated_engines.
    
        Append chrome.ob and chrome.rb to omnibox and realbox search queries
        through the prepopulated engines (TemplateURL flow).
    
        Previously this was done through appending the source param in the
        AutocompleteController flow when opening a match, however it is more
        safe to add this specifically to the google DSE (since that's the only
        place the param is wanted) and to use TemplateURL replacement to achieve
        this. This is removed in this CL.
    
        Trying to append it in the AutocompleteController flow was causing major
        regressions last time (crbug.com/497828304) since it was not being
        appended correctly, this method is more error prone.
    
        Prepopulated engines change rolled over here: crrev.com/c/7837020
    
        NO_IFTTT=This file doesn't exist anymore
    
        Change-Id: I096e608c829658ef84c50c3c367a86448a7b518c
        Bug: 497828304
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7811001
        Reviewed-by: Eva Su <evasu@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Orin Jaworski <orinj@chromium.org>
        Commit-Queue: Nihar Majmudar <niharm@google.com>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1631547}

commit 293ff124dc0b668a3b8e1acf7067d6c3ff4bf792
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 21 17:28:26 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Add new dep for //c/b:global_keyboard_shortcuts_mac
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/a3e448d15eaf9ac752f7e558a3c2f8a4ecb13046
    
    commit a3e448d15eaf9ac752f7e558a3c2f8a4ecb13046
    Author: Erik Chen <erikchen@chromium.org>
    Date:   Tue May 19 11:42:00 2026 -0700
    
        Reland 1: Remove circular dependencies from //chrome/browser:browser
    
        The initial CL was reverted as a suspect for crbug.com/502732679. The
        issue was unrelated and was eventually fixed by crrev.com/c/7858054.
    
        This CL is unchanged from the original CL.
    
        > Remove circular dependencies from //chrome/browser:browser
        >
        > This CL modularizes `//chrome/browser/BUILD.gn` by extracting many
        > header files into separate header-only `source_set` targets (e.g.,
        > `certificate_viewer`, `chrome_browser_main`, `icon_manager`,
        > `process_singleton`, `app_controller_mac`, etc.). This allows downstream
        > targets to depend on individual headers without pulling in the entire
        > `:browser` monolith, and eliminates the large
        > `allow_circular_includes_from` list on the `:browser` target. Downstream
        > `BUILD.gn` files across `chrome/` are updated to depend on the new
        > fine-grained targets, and a number of Android-specific `#include`
        > directives are annotated with `// nogncheck crbug.com/40147906`.
        >
        > AGENT_GENERATED_CL
        >

Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 21 19:01:25 2026 +0100

    [cr150] `Nigori` instantiate requires a keypass
    
    There is a keypass for test code.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/d77c428d50b80d22830c5f39fd55aa49a6c7b5f3
    
    commit d77c428d50b80d22830c5f39fd55aa49a6c7b5f3
    Author: Mikel Astiz <mastiz@chromium.org>
    Date:   Thu May 21 04:46:37 2026 -0700
    
        [sync] Encapsulate Nigori construction in NigoriKeyBag
    
        This patch continues the refactoring series to improve encapsulation and
        decouple the core Sync codebase from internal crypto primitives. It
        focuses on moving the responsibility of Nigori object creation into the
        NigoriKeyBag class and consolidating decryption logic in the bridge.
    
        Key changes:
    
        1. Refactored NigoriKeyBag API:
           - Introduced an overloaded AddKey() method that accepts
             KeyDerivationParams and a password, internalizing the call to
             Nigori::CreateByDerivation().
           - Made the direct AddKey(std::unique_ptr<Nigori>) method private,
             ensuring that all external callers provide the raw data
             (passphrase, params, or proto) rather than pre-instantiated
             crypto objects.
           - Simplified AddKeyFromProto() to leverage the new internal factory.
    
        2. General cleanup and decoupling:
           - Updated CryptographerImpl and KeystoreKeysCryptographer to use the
             new NigoriKeyBag factory methods.
           - Systematically updated unit tests to align with the simplified
             API, further reducing the exposure of Nigori factory methods
             outside the nigori component.
    
        This refactoring further isolates the Nigori implementation details
        within its own component and provides a more robust and idiomatic API
        for the Sync engine (including Nigori bridge).
    
        Bug: 513279006
        Change-Id: Iec4215744638c665d47579f783cf2c83ba54ae73
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7849430
        Commit-Queue: Mikel Astiz <mastiz@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Mahmoud Rashad <mmrashad@google.com>

        [context-menu] Pass tabs from RB/OB AIM entrypoints to Cobrowse
    
        TLDR: This CL associates selected tabs ids with a task so that they can
        be passed from an entrypoint to cobrowse before submission is fully
        done. These tab ids are then used to display the appropriate favicons to
        the user in the "+" button and context menu.
    
        Demo Omnibox:
        http://screencast/cast/NTE1NjYxOTkzNDQ5ODgxNnxhOTM1MzU4Yi1iZQ
    
        Demo NTP: http://screencast/cast/NjEyMzM1Mzg4OTgzMjk2MHxmODQwM2NiMC1jNw
    
        Detailed Implementation:
        - Add `selected_tab_ids_` to `ContextualSearchWebContentsHelper` to store tab IDs associated with a specific task ID.
        - Add `SetRestoredTabIds` to `searchbox.mojom`, allowing the browser to inform the WebUI about tabs that were previously selected for a task.
        - The Browser retrieves tab IDs on initialization to sync UI state.
        - The WebUI now lets `ComposeboxMixin` handle restored tabs and
        refresh suggestions accordingly. It also updates the
        `ContextualActionMenu` to disable and mark as checked the restored tabs.
        It also disables the "Recent tab" text (greying it out).

    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/1ad530fed4cc6bac6878884c223c85533dceef33
    
    commit 1ad530fed4cc6bac6878884c223c85533dceef33
    Author: manukh <manukh@chromium.org>
    Date:   Wed May 20 09:09:08 2026 -0700
    
        [omnibox][next] Use cursor position for autocompletion
    
        Cursor position is an `AutocompleteInput` field. It can affect the
        results for inputs such as:
        - 'youquery|' suggests 'query you'
        - 'you|query' suggests 'your query'
        - 'therm engineering|' suggests 'therm engineering services'
        - 'therm| engineering' suggests 'thermal engineering'
        - 'do butter drink blood|' suggests 'do butter drink blood marry'
        - 'do butter| drink blood' suggests 'do butterflies drink blood'
    
        This field is set in the views omnibox, but not in the realbox,
        composebox, or full webUI omnibox.
    
        This CL wires in cursor position to autocompletion.
    
        Bug: b:512984355
        Change-Id: Ibb4e77fb019ebebccb9923f6b5df8ff45b476168
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7846715

    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/4abe9bf9f06873e7eb520ef94ae8fc9109d75aa4
    
    commit 4abe9bf9f06873e7eb520ef94ae8fc9109d75aa4
    Author: Dana Fried <dfried@chromium.org>
    Date:   Wed May 20 15:56:46 2026 -0700
    
        [Split Tabs] Rename enums to match accepted terminology
    
        Previously, the two split modes were called "horizontal" and "vertical",
        which were confusing because this referred not to the arrangement of the
        contents views, but rather, the orientation of the separator, which was
        not universally intuitive.
    
        The accepted names for these modes are "side by side" and "stacked".
        This CL renames the enum values in both C++ and Mojo to reflect these
        official terms, eliminating ambiguity.
    
        Change-Id: I9da11f91df0bb682070dd67b90b328c48768bc82
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7865208

    Author: Kunal Daftari <kunaldaftari@google.com>
    Date:   Wed May 20 17:14:44 2026 -0700
    
        [SplitTabRestore] Implementing Tab Restore After Restart
    
        This change allows the tab restore system to restore split tabs after
        restarts or browser crashes.
    
        An example flow for testing this is: create a split view, close it,
        restart the browser, ctrl + shift + t.
    
        Notably, this change is not guarded by the flag. This is because it is
        disjoint from the earlier logic of creating the
        `tab_restore::Type::SPLIT` type and we are not allowed to include the
        features file in the components directory.
    
        Two (connected) tests were added:
        - SplitTabRestoreTest.PRE_RestoreSplitAfterRestart
        - SplitTabRestoreTest.RestoreSplitAfterRestart
        to verify this change.
    
        Additionally, there was an edge case where when a tab could not persist
        it would still remain part of the split view. These two test cases were
        added to verify it should return as just a normal tab in that case.
        - SplitTabRestoreTest.PRE_RestoreSplitWithUnpersistableTab
        - SplitTabRestoreTest.RestoreSplitWithUnpersistableTab
    
        This change only applies to normal bulk tab closure. There are still
        edge cases to be worked on w/ tab groups, both open and closed.
    
        Bug: 510426627
        Change-Id: Icaf296895ba93ca8dd72b244732c702b5ebc8f8c

        [actor] TabObservationStrategy 2/4
    
        This CL consumes a TabObservationStrategy to determine whether to
        observe screenshots and DOM content after taking actions.
    
        This object is added in CL 1/4 and populated in CL 3/4.
    
        Specifically, this CL:
        - Adds feature flags kActorObserveScreenshotDefault and kActorObservePageContentDefault to control default observation behavior.
        - Plumbs TabObservationStrategy through ExecutionEngine, ActorTask, ActorKeyedService, and GlicActorTaskManager.
        - Updates TabObservationController to omit screenshot and/or page content fetching based on the strategy and feature flags, skipping observation entirely if both are omitted.
        - Adds comprehensive browsertest coverage verifying the omitting logic.
    
        Design doc:
        https://docs.google.com/document/d/e/2PACX-1vTdL72O0gZRqFaApvSwxtmLPvk9Tyyq-7nfsC9T5IH5zqA7GYZV4nE34yA_FjA5xKIK-GhAc39hDjfO/pub

    Author: Erik Chen <erikchen@chromium.org>
    Date:   Tue May 19 11:42:00 2026 -0700
    
        Reland 1: Remove circular dependencies from //chrome/browser:browser
    
        The initial CL was reverted as a suspect for crbug.com/502732679. The
        issue was unrelated and was eventually fixed by crrev.com/c/7858054.
    
        This CL is unchanged from the original CL.
    
        > Remove circular dependencies from //chrome/browser:browser
        >
        > This CL modularizes `//chrome/browser/BUILD.gn` by extracting many
        > header files into separate header-only `source_set` targets (e.g.,
        > `certificate_viewer`, `chrome_browser_main`, `icon_manager`,
        > `process_singleton`, `app_controller_mac`, etc.). This allows downstream
        > targets to depend on individual headers without pulling in the entire
        > `:browser` monolith, and eliminates the large
        > `allow_circular_includes_from` list on the `:browser` target. Downstream
        > `BUILD.gn` files across `chrome/` are updated to depend on the new
        > fine-grained targets, and a number of Android-specific `#include`
        > directives are annotated with `// nogncheck crbug.com/40147906`.
        >
        > AGENT_GENERATED_CL
        >
        > Bug: 353332589
        > Change-Id: Iedfb2bcbb9530c70cd24db1754960f60d00ab591

commit a254b4dfcd3b95f3907ebbb98d6d650496606b26
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 21 13:54:52 2026 +0100

    [cr150] `OnPassphraseRequired` requires `RequiredPassphraseVerifier`
    
    The arguments stay the same, but now they get passed first to a
    `RequiredPassphraseVerifier` instance, and into this function.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/29093e11cf509e3593f6229e4b1b075cca356049
    
    commit 29093e11cf509e3593f6229e4b1b075cca356049
    Author: Mikel Astiz <mastiz@chromium.org>
    Date:   Tue May 19 07:41:11 2026 -0700
    
        [sync] Avoid direct Nigori dependency in SyncServiceCrypto
    
        Refactoring without user-noticeable behavioral changes (but not a pure
        refactoring strictly speaking; more details below).
    
        With this patch, Nigori-related operations are now encapsulated inside
        SyncEngine, so SyncServiceCrypto doesn't need to be Nigori-aware.
    
        After the recent https://crrev.com/c/7849362, the main remaining
        use-case where SyncServiceCrypto required building Nigori keys was to
        synchronously determine whether or not a user-entered passphrase was
        correct.
    
        To achieve this, class RequiredPassphraseVerifier is introduced, which
        offers precisely this functionality but can be instantiated inside the
        Sync engine (where the code is Nigori-aware).
    
        While functionally equivalent to the previous implementation, there are
        two minor behavioral changes:
        1. Removal of synchronous bootstrap token updates: previously,
           SyncServiceCrypto::SetDecryptionPassphrase() immediately and
           synchronously updated the bootstrap token upon successfully
           verifying the passphrase. Now, it only verifies the passphrase and
           relies on the asynchronous OnPassphraseAccepted() notification from
           the Sync sequence to update the token.
    
        2. For the case where the user enters a successful passphrase, the
           key derivation logic is now exercised twice. This can be a
           performance regression, but the scenario is very rarely exercised
           and the additional CPU time affecting the Sync sequence, so it is
           considered negligible.
    
        Change-Id: I68d8305bd52a1fe21938f94ec105bc7297ff0256
        Bug: 513279006
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7851146
        Reviewed-by: Mahmoud Rashad <mmrashad@google.com>
        Commit-Queue: Mikel Astiz <mastiz@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1632859}

    [cr150] `GetOffTheRecordBrowsersActiveForProfile` deleted

        that no longer have any callers:
    
          - chrome::GetIncognitoBrowserCount()
          - chrome::GetOffTheRecordBrowsersActiveForProfile()

        GetBrowserCount(), which still exists, instead of one of the removed

commit 99cb7afc141a8bdf218be3bcc1b110636d98dc63
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 21 13:33:16 2026 +0100

    [cr150][eslint] Settings code migrated off `any`
    
    This change fixes dozens of `@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any` errors
    that started to happen since the last batch of upstream changes for this
    linting rule.
    
    A few things we had to do in this change:
    
      - `declare prefs: {[key: string]: any}` -> `Record<string, unknown>`,
        matching the upstream substitution in *_page_index.ts files.
      - Extend the global `Window` interface (centralised in
        add_wallet_network_dialog.ts) with typed `testing` and `loadTimeData`
        fields; drop the `(window as any)` casts and use bracket access
        required by noPropertyAccessFromIndexSignature.
      - Replace `this as any` (used to reach private members of the upstream
        parent class) with `this as unknown as { ...specific shape... }` so
        dot access still works.
      - Give the Tor, search-engines and adblock browser proxies real
        interfaces instead of `Promise<any>`.
      - Type Polymer / Leo event handlers with `Event`,
        `Event & {model: {index: number}}`, `CustomEvent<{value: string}>`,
        or local `LeoInputEvent` / `LeoToggleEvent` aliases. Leo's svelte-web
        wrapper forwards the event detail as the event payload itself, hence
        the `{value, valueAsNumber, checked}` shape rather than `.detail.*`.
      - Replace `import('/path' as any)` with a string-variable indirection
        so TS no longer tries to resolve the absolute path statically.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/9b7344de9dcf80545c188e668dd178902cfe7750
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/04f7b4d2ec23e627e3fa25d47793cef99e715615

commit c864bf60a7daadaf310e15653627974600065cf2
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 21 00:46:26 2026 +0100

    [cr150] https://crrev.com/c/7806654 reverted
    
    This has now landed in M150.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/6dae1f10a1fa76a27d771f13e0394fe135940ce3
    
    commit 6dae1f10a1fa76a27d771f13e0394fe135940ce3
    Author: Patrick Monette <pmonette@chromium.org>
    Date:   Mon May 11 19:27:31 2026 -0700
    
        Android: Disable the PrerenderHostRegistry memory pressure listener
    
        A recent'ish refactoring removed
        MemoryPressureMonitor::GetCurrentPressureLevel() in favor of
        MemoryPressureListener::memory_pressure_level().
    
        Although I initially thought that both were equivalent, there is a
        subtle difference on Android, where GetCurrentPressureLevel() used to
        ignore notifications received from MemoryPressureMonitor.java.
    
        This was probably a bug, but the effect of that change is that code that
        relied on GetCurrentPressureLevel() is now being told it is under memory
        pressure more often.
    
        PrerenderHostRegistry is one such case, where the increase in memory
        pressure is undesirable.
    
        Bug: 510968973
        Change-Id: I761018200fef5db30ff10298bce5ccece0a02ae8
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7806654

        Commit-Queue: Hiroki Nakagawa <nhiroki@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1628980}

    commit d515619614a63a92e92854314ef2fcdf04cec82c
    Author: Antonio Sartori <antoniosartori@chromium.org>
    Date:   Tue May 19 05:15:34 2026 -0700
    
        [permissions] Differentiate geolocation prompt variants in UMA
    
        This CL updates a number of permissions UMA metrics to keep track of
        the different kinds of geolocation prompts (when approximate
        geolocation is enabled) separately.
    
        The three kinds of geolocation prompts we currently implement when
        approximate geolocation is enabled are:
        - approximate only
        - approximate/precise
        - upgrade from approximate to precise
    
        Note that this only makes sense for metrics tied to a prompt. For a
        number of other metrics (e.g. permission usage, permission revocation)
        the distinction does not make sense.

    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/11382d95d14ce6a9676ae5079b1e2e358cedb905
    
    commit 11382d95d14ce6a9676ae5079b1e2e358cedb905
    Author: Mikel Astiz <mastiz@chromium.org>
    Date:   Mon May 18 03:29:04 2026 -0700
    
        [sync] Wrap bootstrap token in CustomPassphraseBootstrapToken
    
        Believed to be a pure refactoring without behavioral changes, but
        it is hard to be 100% sure.
    
        Introduces CustomPassphraseBootstrapToken class under
        components/sync/base/ wrapping the concept of bootstrap tokens, which
        in the end is sync_pb::NigoriKey proto. This improves code readability,
        type safety and encapsulation across component boundaries.
    
        Refactors several layers including SyncPrefs, SyncUserSettingsImpl and
        SyncServiceCrypto to avoid strings and use this class instead, which
        disambiguates whether or not those strings are encrypted or
        base64-encoded.
    
        The class exposes dedicated APIs tailored to the specific cases where
        the token is treated as a non-opaque payload, minimizing the risk for
        abuse. For storage in prefs, it internally enforces that OSCrypt is
        used to encrypt and decrypt.
    
        Bug: 513279006
        Change-Id: I3c2dc5b11df7fe74442634a16d63aedc2cc58878
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7852318
        Reviewed-by: Mahmoud Rashad <mmrashad@google.com>
        Commit-Queue: Mikel Astiz <mastiz@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1632057}

        Restore focus after same-process print popup tab close

commit cedb49dc2e5dbe9e7ecbbcb8b4883959d2ea8f44
Author: AlexeyBarabash <alexey@brave.com>
Date:   Tue May 19 00:23:50 2026 +0300

    [cr150][Android] Fix VerifyError in TabImpl.initWebContents
    
    R8 inlines DeferredContentViewStub.<init> (which calls super() →
    ContentView.<init>) into initWebContents and incorrectly inserts a
    check-cast on the uninitialized reference before invoke-direct <init>,
    causing a VerifyError on tab restore in release arm64 builds.
    
    The bug is triggered by Brave's extra ProGuard keep rules shifting R8's
    whole-program inlining decisions compared to Chromium's build.
    
    Fix: keep DeferredContentViewStub.<init> in proguard.flags so R8 treats
    it as an external entry point and does not inline it.

commit 02f9274c45fd59cd000adc6773c4f43cc2f2fb6a
Author: AlexeyBarabash <alexey@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 15 20:30:04 2026 +0300

    [cr150][Android] Skip GetContentSetting for PermissionSettings-only types
    
    OnContentSettingChanged's predicate calls GetContentSetting to check whether
    the current setting differs from the stored value. GetContentSetting CHECKs
    the type is in ContentSettingsRegistry. GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS is registered
    only in PermissionSettingsRegistry, so the predicate crashes when a geolocation
    setting change notification is processed on Android with
    kApproximateGeolocationPermission enabled.
    
    Fix: skip the GetContentSetting comparison for types not in
    ContentSettingsRegistry. ContentSettingsPref only fires the notification when
    the value actually changed, so a pattern match alone is sufficient to remove
    the expiration. PLM's own resets are already guarded by
    is_currently_removing_permissions_.
    
    Chromium change:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/96d8c5eb0773a93cf85aeb73e97c822c379c8d26
    
    commit 96d8c5eb0773a93cf85aeb73e97c822c379c8d26
    Author: Antonio Sartori <antoniosartori@chromium.org>
    Date:   Thu May 7 10:48:35 2026 -0700
    
        [permissions] Enable kApproximateGeolocationPermission on Android
    
        Bug: b:385175104
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1627060}

    [cr150][Android] Fix ResetPermission crash for GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS
    
    SetContentSettingDefaultScope CHECKs the type is in ContentSettingsRegistry.
    GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS is registered only in PermissionSettingsRegistry, so
    calling ResetPermission when a geolocation lifetime expires crashes on Android
    with kApproximateGeolocationPermission enabled.

commit bd0d73059046b490a73b12abe39093016ce0f8eb
Author: AlexeyBarabash <alexey@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 15 19:51:29 2026 +0300

    [cr150][Android] Geolocation accuracy option at permission dialog
    
    Implements a Precise/Approximate radio button group in Brave's Android
    permission dialog for GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS requests (i.e. when
    kApproximateGeolocationPermission is enabled).
    
    Previously the dialog defaulted unconditionally to kPrecise to avoid a
    CHECK crash in GeolocationPermissionResolver. Now:
    
    - C++ detects GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS in BravePreCreateDialog and sets
      a flag on BravePermissionDialogDelegate via JNI.
    - Java adds a "Location precision" label with Precise / Approximate
      radio buttons above the "Remember my decision" lifetime selector.
    - The user's choice is read back in BRAVE_PERMISSION_DIALOG_DELEGATE_ACCEPT
      via GetGeolocationAccuracy() and used to populate GeolocationPromptOptions,
      replacing the previous hardcoded kPrecise default.
    
    UI polish: added 16dp top margin to both the "Location precision" and
    "Remember my decision" labels so they don't run flush against the
    permission message text above them.
    
    Verification:
    - Enable kApproximateGeolocationPermission (default on Android).
    - Visit a site that requests geolocation (e.g. maps.google.com).
    - Precise/Approximate radio group appears above the lifetime selector.
    - Selecting Approximate and allowing grants approximate location
      (visible as "Allowed • Approximate" in Site Settings).

    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/96d8c5eb0773a93cf85aeb73e97c822c379c8d26

commit 72384664587ffd00a7e9f4d39933092e028d1836
Author: AlexeyBarabash <alexey@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 15 16:48:37 2026 +0300

    [cr150][Android] kApproximateGeolocationPermission enabled on Android
    
    Fix PermissionLifetimeManagerTest.ExternalContentSettingChange:
    PermissionDecided stores expirations under the type returned by
    GeolocationContentSettingsType() — which is GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS on
    Android — while SetContentSettingDefaultScope fires notifications for plain
    GEOLOCATION. OnContentSettingChanged found nothing in expirations keyed
    under GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS and returned early without stopping the timer.
    Using GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS directly in the test also crashes: it is
    registered only in PermissionSettingsRegistry::Init(), never through
    ContentSettingsRegistry::Register(), so GetContentSetting() hits NOTREACHED
    via CheckContentTypeRegistration → ContentSettingsRegistry::Get().
    Fix: switch ExternalContentSettingChange to ContentSettingsType::NOTIFICATIONS
    which has no platform-specific aliasing and tests the same PLM observer
    behaviour end-to-end.
    
    Fix PermissionLifetimeManagerTest.DifferentTypePermissions:
    Same root cause — GEOLOCATION maps to GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS on Android,
    causing a pref key mismatch ("geolocation-with-options" vs "geolocation") and
    a CHECK crash in ResetPermission when the expiration timer fires:
    SetContentSettingDefaultScope CHECKs the type is in ContentSettingsRegistry
    but GEOLOCATION_WITH_OPTIONS is not.
    Fix: replace GEOLOCATION with ContentSettingsType::MEDIASTREAM_MIC (pref name
    "media-stream-mic"), which has no Android aliasing and is in
    ContentSettingsRegistry.

    [cr150][bedrock] `FindTabbedBrowser` and others deleted

    Author: Yu He <yhe@microsoft.com>
    Date:   Sun May 17 22:10:11 2026 -0700
    
        [bedrock] Remove legacy chrome::Find* and GetTotalBrowserCount helpers
    
        Deletes five free functions from chrome/browser/ui/browser_finder.{h,cc}
        that have been superseded by ProfileBrowserCollection and
        GlobalBrowserCollection:
    
          - chrome::FindTabbedBrowser
          - chrome::FindBrowserWithProfile
          - chrome::FindLastActiveWithProfile
          - chrome::FindLastActive
          - chrome::GetTotalBrowserCount
    
        Remaining callsites are migrated to the new APIs:
    
          - chrome::GetTotalBrowserCount()
              -> GlobalBrowserCollection::GetInstance()->GetSize()
          - chrome::FindBrowserWithProfile(profile)
              -> ProfileBrowserCollection::GetForProfile(profile)
                     ->GetLastActiveBrowser()
                (with a null check on GetForProfile())
    
        The browser_window_features() pointer accessor is also replaced with the
        BrowserWindowInterface::GetFeatures() reference accessor at the migrated
        callsite.
    
        Also drops the FindTabbedBrowser browser test, the now-unused
        BrowserWindowInterface forward declaration and
        ui/display/types/display_constants.h include from the header, and
        several dead includes from the touched .cc files (<algorithm>,
        tab_contents_iterator.h, navigation_controller.h, browser_view.h,
        browser_finder.h).
    
        No behavior change.

    [gnrt][rust][cr150] Fixing `readme.rs` patches to `get_license_files`

    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/47669f57b5872ae0ca4d3a2ec552c17962527828
    
    commit 47669f57b5872ae0ca4d3a2ec552c17962527828
    Author: Lukasz Anforowicz <lukasza@chromium.org>
    Date:   Fri May 15 14:43:21 2026 -0700
    
        [gnrt] Require *each* license kind to have a separate license file.
    
        Before this CL `gnrt` would only check that any license files were
        found.  This could result in a situation where only 1 of 2 required
        license kinds would have an associated license file.
    
        After this CL the license file checks are more robust.  The CL also
        added unit test coverage for the license files (make this area of code
        more testable by refactoring it into a separate function).  In
        particular, `test_get_license_files_two_licenses_one_file_missing`
        checks that the problem from https://crbug.com/511849153 should now be
        detected early.
