commit c74e56eaca30c55d82032ab104c596a14bb9a6f9
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Mon May 18 11:43:24 2026 +0100

    [plaster][cr150] `//third_party/blink/renderer/modules` migrated
    
    Migrating this patch as this was causing unnecessary merge conflicts.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/b676377adb9788d2b1788fe83e3b904db6c2225a
    
    commit b676377adb9788d2b1788fe83e3b904db6c2225a
    Author: Evan liu <evliu@google.com>
    Date:   Fri May 15 16:30:29 2026 -0700
    
        Fix Web Speech API socket leak when using MediaStreamTrack
    
        When `SpeechRecognition::start(MediaStreamTrack*)` is called, a
        `SpeechRecognitionMediaStreamAudioSink` is created and registered to
        the track. However, this sink was never unregistered when the
        recognition session ended or aborted.
    
        Over multiple start/stop cycles, this caused a severe resource leak
        where sinks accumulated indefinitely, eventually exhausting Mojo IPC
        limits and causing persistent 'network' errors.
    
        This CL fixes the leak by tracking the audio sink in
        `SpeechRecognition` and properly unregistering and removing it from
        the `MediaStreamTrack` when `SpeechRecognition::Ended()` is called.
    
        Fixed: 497276218
        Change-Id: I4d8c5a98e7b5fe242a3caeb333585f5d1395c35b
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7850843
        Reviewed-by: Elad Alon <eladalon@chromium.org>
        Commit-Queue: Evan Liu <evliu@google.com>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1631628}

commit 0c971b53f6c904ef2bfc0cdcb8edc9565c8555ea
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>

    [cr150] Stubbing off `OnEmbeddedPermissionPromptChanged`
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/03d0729142a7f3db6bc6a16d69de16832cf32320
    
    commit 03d0729142a7f3db6bc6a16d69de16832cf32320
    Author: James Leung <jamesleung@google.com>
    Date:   Thu May 14 22:43:43 2026 -0700
    
        [voice_search] Keep voice search open during permission prompt
    
        Modify the composebox voice search to remain active when an embedded
        permission prompt is displayed. This prevents the voice search overlay
        from timing out or closing while the user interacts with system access
        requests. An observer must be added to communicate via mojo to the
        frontend when the voice search should remain active.
    
        Key changes include:
        * Implemented `EmbeddedPermissionPromptObserver` to track the
          lifecycle and bounds of the embedded permission prompt widget. When
          it resizes, closes due to out of focus, or closes due to an option
          being selected, it sends a mojo message (`OnEmbeddedPermissionPromptChanged`)
        * Added a new Mojo method `OnEmbeddedPermissionPromptChanged`
          to tell the frontend when the permission prompt is visible,
          and the prompt's size
        * Made page callback passed down to `cr-composebox-voice-search`. Also
          made it protected instead of private.
        * Updated `cr-composebox-voice-search` to listen for permission state
            changes, effectively pausing the idle timer when the permission
            prompt is visible.
    
        screencast/cast/NTU0NDc5Mjc3MDQ3ODA4MHxiYzc3ZmYyYy1hNQ
        NO_IFTTT=just rearranged and made existing property protected
        It is known that it should be moved to mixin.

    [cr150] Drop `chromium_src` override for `history_url_visit_data_fetcher_unittest.cc`
    
    Upstream replaced `MockDeviceInfoTracker` with `syncer::FakeDeviceInfoTracker`,
    so there is no longer a mock subclass into which we need to inject
    `GetAllBraveDeviceInfo()`. Our existing `FakeDeviceInfoTracker` override already
    supplies that method, making this test override redundant.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/50f3b26aa894e332fb42ac43d970e940868a6eef
    
    commit 50f3b26aa894e332fb42ac43d970e940868a6eef
    Author: Mikel Astiz <mastiz@chromium.org>
    Date:   Wed May 13 07:39:11 2026 -0700
    
        [visited-url-ranking] Simplify tests dealing with syncer::DeviceInfo
    
        This patch refactors HistoryURLVisitDataFetcherTest to use standard sync
        test fakes instead of manual mocks, making the tests more robust and
        readable.
    
        Among other benefits, the manual construction of syncer::DeviceInfo is
        avoided, allowing this signature to change without having to update
        unrelated tests.
    
        The patch includes:
        1. Removed custom MockDeviceInfoTracker and MockDeviceInfoSyncService
           implementations.
    
        2. Adopted syncer::FakeDeviceInfoSyncService instead, which comes with
           syncer::FakeDeviceInfoTracker.
    
        3. Removed the global kSampleForeignDeviceInfo variable (violating
           Google C++ style guide for non-trivial destructors) and replaced it
           with inline usage of syncer::TestDeviceInfoBuilder (which avoids
           calling DeviceInfo's constructor directly).
    
        4. Simplified SetDeviceInfoTrackerExpectations and other test setup logic
           by directly populating the fake tracker.
    
        5. Cleaned up includes (IWYU).
    
        Bug: 510816366
        Change-Id: I22dd3113d7561062e8fd99dcbb40cd345e6e1797

commit 90466f1cf13a0f6a29a18a5054fa5dc84ebc72b6
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 14 10:10:14 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Fix `CustomizeChromeSidePanelBrowserTest` grabbing wrong `WebContents`
    
    `SidePanelUI::GetWebContentsForTest` calls `SidePanelEntry::GetContent()`, whose
    move-out semantics re-run the entry's content factory when the live view is
    already attached to the panel. That produced a parallel hidden
    `WebUIContentsWrapperT<CustomizeChromeUI>` whose navigation no longer reaches
    `DidStopLoading` on cr150, so `WaitForLoadStop` timed out at 30s.
    
    Grab the live side-panel WebContents from the view hierarchy via
    `SidePanelWebUIView::kSidePanelWebViewId` instead.
    
    Note: AI-assisted: requires thorough review

commit 43894fd8cc6e48592d8a2cf671271959702cd11b
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Wed May 13 18:31:23 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Drop Web Store from `CheckExpectedExtensions`
    
    Upstream gates the Web Store hosted app behind
    `extensions_features::kWebstoreHostedApp`, which is disabled by default
    everywhere except ChromeOS, so ComponentLoader::AddWebStoreApp() no longer
    installs kWebStoreAppId on desktop. Remove it from `expected_extensions` in
    `BraveContentBrowserClientTest.CheckExpectedExtensions` to match the new default
    as the upstream code comment says that the next step is to remove the flag
    completely.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/22c9e8a880dfbfbb456e40ffd37c60309e79faaa
    
    commit 22c9e8a880dfbfbb456e40ffd37c60309e79faaa
    Author: Devlin Cronin <rdevlin.cronin@chromium.org>
    Date:   Fri May 8 17:55:07 2026 -0700
    
        [Extensions] Stop loading the webstore component hosted app on non-CrOS
    
        The webstore hosted app is a component item that used to be necessary as
        an implementation detail to both isolate the old webstore and expose the
        webstorePrivate API to it. This was necessary when the webstore was at
        chrome.google.com/webstore, since this wasn't an origin boundary (and we
        wanted to treat that site differently from other chrome.google.com
        sites).
    
        Since the webstore is now at chromewebstore.google.com, this is no
        longer necessary. The webstore hosted app can be safely removed from
        most builds. The exception (for now) is ChromeOS, where the webstore
        hosted app also serves to add a quick launch icon for the store.
    
        This CL adds a new base::Feature to control loading the webstore hosted
        app. It is default-enabled (i.e., hosted app is loaded) on ChromeOS and
        default disabled (hosted app is not loaded) on non-ChromeOS. This gives
        us a killswitch in case anything goes terribly wrong.
    
        A few tests have to be updated as a part of this, since they had
        expectations around the behavior of chrome.google.com/webstore, which
        now (by design) only holds true for ChromeOS platforms.
    
        Bug: 328494022
        Change-Id: I3c135a900e52e879f03f4e25698b345ab256dd10
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7804680
        Reviewed-by: Charlie Reis <creis@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Maksim Moskvitin <mmoskvitin@google.com>
        Commit-Queue: Devlin Cronin <rdevlin.cronin@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Tim <tjudkins@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1628045}

commit d42a80bcb7dc8f9ff28c6a7d4b5d13f8c6029c28
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Wed May 13 18:22:27 2026 -0400

    [cr150] Override `MultiContentsView::SetSplitViewInsets` to keep zero padding
    
    Upstream now calls `MultiContentsView::SetSplitViewInsets` on every layout pass
    while in split view, applying `kSplitViewContentInset` to the left/right edges
    of the split contents views and defeating `BraveMultiContentsView`'s
    constructor-time zeroing and breaking
    `SidebarBrowserWithSplitViewTest.ShowSidebarOnMouseOverTest` by pushing the left
    split view past the sidebar hot corner.
    
    To address this, we create an override in `BraveMultiContentsView` to always
    forward zero insets to the base class.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/c17558320de2c559263397bbfa447bb6383adf89

commit 432b36f8e72ac223c36f8748a4ee922e4a5eba08
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Tue May 5 01:23:47 2026 +0100

    [cr150] Drop obsolete `close_button_` reorder workaround in `BraveConfirmInfoBar`
    
    Found the real cause. The flex-layout commit was in M149, but it was gated behind the kInfobarRefresh feature
    
    The `kInfobarRefresh` feature flag was removed and `InfoBarView`'s `FlexLayout`
    path is permanently enabled now. This keeps `close_button_` inside
    `right_side_container_` instead of as a direct child of `InfoBarView`. That made
    `BraveConfirmInfoBar`'s `ReorderChildView(close_button_, ...)` trip the
    `view->parent_ == this` `DCHECK` in `views::View::ReorderChildView`, crashing every
    test that constructs a `BraveConfirmInfoBar`.
    
    The flex layout's `right_side_container_` already keeps the close button
    visually last, so the workaround and its `CloseButtonOrderTest` are removed.
    
    Chromium change:
    https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/69e4d3378e4255aa94f5fb56cbd378a5bbe6ffed
    
    commit 69e4d3378e4255aa94f5fb56cbd378a5bbe6ffed
    Author: Foromo Daniel Soromou <koretadaniel@chromium.org>
    Date:   Tue May 5 11:40:38 2026 -0700
    
        [Cleanup] Remove kInfobarRefresh feature flag
    
        Remove the kInfobarRefresh feature flag and permanently enable the
        refreshed infobar UI and FlexLayout-based design.
    
        This cleanup involves the following changes:
        * Deletes the kInfobarRefresh feature from ui_features.
        * Removes old absolute-positioning layout logic and manual coordinate
          calculations from InfoBarView, ConfirmInfoBar, TabSharingInfoBar,
          and AlternateNavInfoBarView.
        * Unconditionally applies FlexLayout properties, refreshed margins,
          paddings, and background colors (ui::kColorSysSurface2) to all
          infobars.
        * Cleans up browser tests by removing outdated parameterizations and
          legacy test cases for the old infobar UI and disabled prioritization
          states.
    
        Bug: 509880510
        Change-Id: Ib3625cc0f3824c6183c1e2b263e58daa50185af8
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7816698

commit 57ccd3c9d09eedf31d90af8934756547cd64e12c
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 9 23:13:31 2026 +0100

    [cr149][WIP] Restoring deleted fields to `WorkerContentSettingsClient`
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/8c04824cab07837e20185e363ad86289b1aace87
    
    commit 8c04824cab07837e20185e363ad86289b1aace87
    Author: Antonio Sartori <antoniosartori@chromium.org>
    Date:   Wed Apr 8 04:04:19 2026 -0700
    
        Remove redundant params from ContentSettingsManager mojo method
    
        This CL removes the parameters origin, site_for_cookies and
        top_frame_origin from ContentSettingsManager::AllowStorageAccess,
        since they can be retrieved from the RenderFrameHost on the browser
        side.
    
        In order to do that, we need to move the mojo implementation to the UI
        thread, where the RenderFrameHost lives. Since the methods post on the
        UI thread anyway, there shouldn't be any performance implications.
        Note that https://crrev.com/c/3062003 moved the
        ContentSettingsManagerImpl off the UI thread in the first place for
        optimization reasons.
    
        It would make sense to further remove the frame_token parameter and
        make the browser implementation associated with the DocumentData, but
        that requires a deeper refactoring since this interface should then be
        extended to workers, too.
    
        Bug: 492968151
        Change-Id: I42015a053fd15794164a84de7abd9ae58b4b686c
        Fixed: 492968151
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7726063

    Author: dpapad <dpapad@chromium.org>
    Date:   Mon Apr 6 20:34:40 2026 -0700
    
        [Reland] WebUI: Update TypeScript compiler from 5.9.3 to 6.0.2.
    
        Reland notes: Revert was caused by a bug in
        @typescript-eslint/typescript-estree v8.58.0 which only triggers in a
        couple post commit bots. The problem was worked around in the precursor
        https://crrev.com/c/7727885.
    
        Specifically:
         - Removing chrome/browser/resources/glic/url_pattern.d.ts since these
           are now part of TS compiler's default definitions.
         - Changing 'module' to 'namespace' in
           components/translate/ios/browser/resources/translate_ios.ts, since
           usage of the deprecated "module" now throws an error [1].
         - Updating third_party/node/patches/typescript.patch to restore the
           type of `HTMLElement#hidden` to just `boolean` instead of
           `"boolean|"until-found"` since the latter causes a lot of TS errors
           in WebUI tests. These will be addressed in a follow-up.
         - Removing newly unnecessary definitions in
           tools/typescript/definitions/pending.d.ts.
    
        CrOS changes
         - Adding 'ignoreDeprecations' flag in CrOS targets that fail otherwise
           due to using stuff that is officially deprecated in v6:
           - chrome/browser/resources/chromeos/accessibility/
           - third_party/cros-components/
           - third_party/material_web_components/
         - Fixing newly surfaced type errors in ash/webui/media_app_ui/ and
           ui/file_manager/
    
        [1] https://devblogs.microsoft.com/typescript/announcing-typescript-6-0/#deprecated:-legacy-module-syntax-for-namespaces

commit d3eddd38cec65e499e32c5bc44c43c5eb41ed0dd
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Tue May 12 14:35:22 2026 +0100

    [cr150] `SetWebsiteSetting` passing `Value` by ref
    
    These interfaces were changed, and it cascaded into our code in quite a
    few places. In one particular case a `Clone()` had to be introduced, as
    the upstream code still takes by value. Trying to fix this in upstream
    has made it clear that things will remain as they are for now.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/41de479be5003693b62fcdf169eccf0af554293a
    
    commit 41de479be5003693b62fcdf169eccf0af554293a
    Author: Antonio Sartori <antoniosartori@chromium.org>
    Date:   Mon May 11 01:30:14 2026 -0700
    
        Convert ContentSettingsProvider::SetWebsiteSetting to const base::Value&
    
        This CL converts ContentSettingsProvider::SetWebsiteSetting to take a
        `const base::Value&` instead of a `base::Value&&`.
    
        This seems to better adhere to the style guide
        (https://google.github.io/styleguide/cppguide.html#Rvalue_references),
        which does not allow using rvalue references excepts in a small number
        of cases, none of which seems to apply in this case.
    
        Note that the C++ linter used to trigger a (non-real) use-after-move
        warning on CLs passing a value by std::move() and then reusing it
        since it was not being consumed by the function. This CL solves that.
    
        Possible alternatives could have been to either pass a `base::Value`
        or a `base::Value&`. The first alternative has been discarded because
        it would need the callers to always pass by value even if in most
        cases SetWebsiteSetting() does not consume the argument. The second
        alternative seems complicated and error-prone (the caller would have
        to remember to check the returned boolean in order to know whether the
        base::Value was consumed or not, which seems like a very likely source
        of bugs), and it would not have supported callers passing a literal
        (Rvalue reference).
    
        Taking a `const base::Value&` seems like the best option, even if it
        sometimes results in the function needing to Clone() the value for
        processing it internally.
    
        Change-Id: I43215b9fc1292470d9be2c3fe1e1241e4b49a98e
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7832363
        Reviewed-by: Dibyajyoti Pal <dibyapal@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: James Lee <ljjlee@google.com>
        Reviewed-by: John Lee <johntlee@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Reilly Grant <reillyg@chromium.org>
        Commit-Queue: Antonio Sartori <antoniosartori@chromium.org>
        Reviewed-by: Christian Dullweber <dullweber@chromium.org>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1628420}

commit b59067d6377f83ef22ca2fdae350787fd9696756
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>

    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/e8fac8e9ac963d6f3f19bd6ba0335af7c7c92e1a
    
    commit e8fac8e9ac963d6f3f19bd6ba0335af7c7c92e1a
    Author: alphonsea@google.com <alphonsea@google.com>
    Date:   Mon May 11 10:05:00 2026 -0700
    
        Add regex dependency for libafl crate usage
    
        Due to the size of crrev.com/c/7564051, this CL works to split all of
        the unsafe dependencies into separate CLs for individual review. The end
        goal is to have all unsafe transitive dependencies for libafl imported
        and reviewed prior to importing the remaining dependencies (including
        libafl). We have approval for importing libafl by Chrome TSCs/ATLs (see

    [cr150][Android] Fix BravePictureInPictureActivity parent after VideoOverlayActivity refactor
    
    Upstream extracted VideoOverlayActivity as a new base class for
    PictureInPictureActivity, moving methods (finishOverlay, hangUp,
    getNativeToken, etc.) there. Brave's bytecode patcher inserts
    BravePictureInPictureActivity between PictureInPictureActivity and
    its upstream parent, but BravePictureInPictureActivity still extended
    AsyncInitializationActivity, breaking the inheritance chain. R8
    flagged the missing method symbols at link time. Update
    BravePictureInPictureActivity to extend VideoOverlayActivity instead.

commit 151f5978a22922cc5eba616c2d0a2554159f1910
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Mon May 11 00:52:33 2026 +0100

    [cr150][plaster] `//components/omnibox/browser` build patch migrated
    
    This particular source is being migrated as it is a case of a frail
    patch, that breaks easily on rebases, and can be easily managed by
    plaster.
    
    The new plaster has broken apart the patching of
    `sources`/`deps`/`public_deps` into three substitutions, because this
    has no additional cost to the plaster effectiveness, but it does help
    with readability as each substitution is put next to what they are
    changing.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/2a2d45627669d484a0fe282db436116cdfcc0c4c
    
    commit 2a2d45627669d484a0fe282db436116cdfcc0c4c
    Author: Wenyu Fu <wenyufu@chromium.org>
    Date:   Fri May 8 13:24:42 2026 -0700
    
        [ContextualTasks] Migrate Desktop Composebox Handler to Android
    
        Migrate `ContextualTasksComposeboxHandler` to Android. This unifies the
        composebox and searchbox C++ backend logic for Contextual Tasks across
        Desktop and Android, enabling Desktop Composebox WebUI reuse on Android.
    
        This is made possible because `TabListInterface` is supported on Android
        via `TabModel`. Lens C++ dependencies which is not supported on Android
        isolated in this CL.
    
        Key changes:
        - Update `BUILD.gn` to compile the handler on Android and remove the
          stub.
        - Update `desktop_query_contextualizer_delegate.cc` to include the
          correct `tab_features.h` header depending on the platform.
        - Update `contextual_tasks_ui.cc` to instantiate the unified
          handler.
        - Guard out Desktop-only `new_tab_page:resources` and
          `sanitized_image_source` on Android to avoid pulling in the
          entire NTP frontend.
    
        The compose box does not render yet.
    
        Preview: https://screenshot.googleplex.com/6hpKQxwoBh6GpHv
        Binary-Size: Pulled in webUI component and resources, unavoidable.
        Bug: b:509722915
        Test: Compile and run chrome_apk

    [cr150] Pass through new insecure_dns param to ConfigureStubHostResolver
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/35047492b52662e99bab37a78297f1b8a946afbe
    
    commit 35047492b52662e99bab37a78297f1b8a946afbe
    Author: Stefano Duo <stefanoduo@google.com>
    Date:   Fri May 8 02:48:25 2026 -0700
    
        Setup experiment flags to use TaskType::DNS_PLATFORM
    
        This targets the following //net's embedders: Chrome on Android, Cronet
        and WebView. The flags are separate to decouple each embedder's rollout.
    
        For Chrome on Android, Cronet and WebView, the flags must:
        1. Make it so the insecure part of the built-in resolver uses
           TaskType::DNS_PLATFORM instead of TaskType::DNS
        2. Fall back onto TaskType::SYSTEM if TaskType::DNS_PLATFORM fails
    
        Additionally, for Cronet and WebView, the flags must also enable the
        insecure part of the built-in resolver.
    
        Bug: 448975408
        Change-Id: I643f3448a9bfbaf882b8e39fb5f90a696afbd5d7
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7532167

commit e9a64cf610bbb9689419c4a59492f854f4245ffc
Author: Emerick Rogul <erogul@brave.com>
Date:   Sat May 9 12:49:33 2026 -0400

    [cr150] `//chrome/browser` split into `:core` and `:browser`
    
    This upstream change moved `defaults.h`, `file_select_helper.h`, and
    `command_observer.h` into the new `source_set("core")`, which
    `brave/browser/ui:ui` can no longer reach. Mirror the existing `:browser`
    injection on `:core` so `brave/browser/ui` participates in :core's
    `allow_circular_includes_from` list.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/6be6fe6fefe6cb1ec11cdb9e74b7d304cd92d094
    
    commit 6be6fe6fefe6cb1ec11cdb9e74b7d304cd92d094
    Author: Erik Chen <erikchen@chromium.org>
    Date:   Thu May 7 23:51:10 2026 -0700
    
        Reland 2: Modularize //chrome/browser
    
        The first reland caused a CI builder failure on mac-rel-cft. This is
        because chrome_browser_main.cc has many conditional includes, some of
        which are only exercised on CI builders. For this reland,
        chrome_browser_main.cc is moved back into the original "browser"
        static_library. mega-cq was run until it passed.
    
        > Reland 1: Modularize //chrome/browser
        >
        > The initial CL did not land cleanly because a high-traffic file
        > about_flags.cc was changed between the successful CQ run and the CL
        > landing. This CL moves about_flags.cc back into unmodularized "browser"
        > static_library for now.
        >
        > > This CL refactors `chrome/browser/BUILD.gn` by splitting the existing
        > > `static_library("browser")` into a new `source_set("core")` target plus
        > > a slimmed-down `static_library("browser")`. The new `:core` target
        > > absorbs the bulk of the source files, deps, and

commit d35dbf23575b25f3d46de1730d70e9a128c9e179
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Sat May 9 13:37:19 2026 +0100

    [cr150] `SiteInstance::GetSiteURL` deleted
    
    This is now supposed to be retrieved as `GetDeprecatedSiteURL` from
    `SecurityPrincipal`.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/01d357ddeead2af7f1b41c2410510d589610b36d
    
    commit 01d357ddeead2af7f1b41c2410510d589610b36d
    Author: Viktoriya Bryhider <vbryhider@microsoft.com>
    Date:   Thu May 7 19:06:15 2026 -0700
    
        Move GetSiteURL to SecurityPrincipal interface
    
        Move the site URL accessor from SiteInstance and SiteInfo into the
        SecurityPrincipal interface as GetDeprecatedSiteURL(). This consolidates
        security-related accessors behind SecurityPrincipal and makes the
        deprecation status of the site URL explicit in the API.
    
        Remove SiteInstance::GetSiteURL() and SiteInfo::site_url(), replacing
        them with SecurityPrincipal::GetDeprecatedSiteURL(). Internal SiteInfo
        code now accesses the site_url_ member directly where appropriate.
    
        Update all callers across chrome/, content/, and extensions/ to use the
        new GetSecurityPrincipal().GetDeprecatedSiteURL() path.
    
        The existing functionality remains unchanged.
    
        Bug: 397481045, 40526490
        Change-Id: I15e60f7d005865428ea5b50f85bbe1606ec04768
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7614138

    Author: Chris Thompson <cthomp@chromium.org>
    Date:   Thu May 7 15:08:20 2026 -0700
    
        Fix ABH bypass for Advanced Protection users
    
        Some ABH Balanced Mode exemptions were incorrectly applying to Advanced
        Protection users after previous changes to how Advanced Protection
        status was applied (in crbug.com/480099712). This fixes this by checking
        IsInterstitialEnabled() and IsStrictInterstitialEnabled() instead of
        querying the underlying pref value in various places (throttle creation
        and when checking exemption status). This also simplifies setup by
        consolidating logic into ComputeInterstitialState().
    
        This also adds a regression test (using the non-default ports
        exemption).

commit 30338598cd084eb28801efc44c1ad209ce583b5b
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 8 14:28:24 2026 +0100

    [cr150] `WebRequestInfo` using `GlobalRenderFrameHostId`
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/0f97ab9a245aad026a65711c9bfc865789d88b3b
    
    commit 0f97ab9a245aad026a65711c9bfc865789d88b3b
    Author: Chris Staite <christopher.staite@menlosecurity.com>
    Date:   Thu May 7 11:43:37 2026 -0700
    
        Migrate WebRequestInfo to use GlobalRenderFrameHostId
    
        This commit replaces the raw integer representations of render process
        and frame routing IDs with the strongly-typed GlobalRenderFrameHostId
        in WebRequestInfo and WebRequestInfoInitParams.
    
        Additionally, it updates WebRequestEventRouter and related permissions
        logic to utilize content::ChildProcessId instead of raw integers.
    
        These changes improve type safety across the Web Request API and remove
        magic number checks (e.g., checking for -1 to identify the browser
        process) in favor of null checks on the typed IDs. This also resolves
        multiple tracking TODOs by removing the need for unsafe value
        conversions (FromUnsafeValue and GetUnsafeValue).
    
        Bug: 379869738
        Change-Id: I55b4ff004962d843b304a80c5e0444a4279ce7de
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7806833
        Reviewed-by: Andrea Orru <andreaorru@chromium.org>
        Commit-Queue: Christopher Staite <christopher.staite@menlosecurity.com>
        Cr-Commit-Position: refs/heads/main@{#1627097}

commit 38357e2cd8b5a64abaf8bd512de0634c0eb5352c
Author: Claudio DeSouza <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 8 14:25:43 2026 +0100

    [cr150] Lifting deleted rss code into `brave_news`
    
    This change lifts the rss code that is being deleted from Chromium. The
    code is being placed under `brave_news/`, as this is the only consumer
    we have.
    
    Chromium changes:
    https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/19de65fe3ff28e4802c6160fadeba15e92162abc
    
    commit 19de65fe3ff28e4802c6160fadeba15e92162abc
    Author: Yanling <yanlinghu@google.com>
    Date:   Thu May 7 07:28:48 2026 -0700
    
        [Feed] Part9 of remove web feed feature: Remove unread content observer and rss related code
    
        This CL continues the deprecation of the Web Feed (Following feed)
        feature by cleaning up orphaned infrastructure and dead code:
    
        1. UnreadContentObserver: Removed `UnreadContentObserver`,
        `JavaUnreadContentObserver`, and their associated JNI bridges. This
        observer was exclusively instantiated and registered for
        `StreamKind.FOLLOWING` to track whether the Web Feed had unread content
        [1]. With Web Feed removed, this observer is never used.
    
        2. RSS Link Fetching: Removed `RssLinksFetcher`,
        `WebFeedPageInformationFetcher`, and the cross-process
        `mojom::RssLinkReader` interface. This pipeline was built exclusively
        for the Web Feeds system to extract RSS/Atom links from the renderer
        process [2]. Because Web Feed was the sole consumer of this Mojo
        interface, the entire fetching infrastructure and its associated
        unit/browser tests are deleted.
    
        3. Histogram: ContentSuggestions.Feed.WebFeed.GetRssLinksRendererTime is
        removed
    
        [1]
        https://drive.google.com/file/d/1VBYqSmyaXK9Kj6qmLkGXDVPGGLm2oBQk/view?usp=sharing&resourcekey=0-y0MHR_JGdIJxGV_iIYYRRg
        [2]
        https://drive.google.com/file/d/1Ctsit3vsgjoHF22KGEoqMp0mbqooukQ9/view?usp=sharing&resourcekey=0-eSIkBHfiuwObsXBa3oiMYA
    
        Cq-Include-Trybots: luci.chrome.try:android-internal-binary-size;luci.chrome.try:android-internal-rel;luci.chrome.try:android-internal-dbg
        Bug: 407797637

    Author: manukh <manukh@chromium.org>
    Date:   Mon May 4 22:34:21 2026 -0700
    
        [omnibox][keyword] Replace AutocompleteInput::keyword_mode_entry_method_
    
        Before, it was an enum representing how the user entered keyword mode
        (e.g. tab, ctrl+k, etc).
    
        Now, it is a boolean `in_keyword_mode_`.
    
        None of the autocomplete consumers cared how keyword mode was entered.
        Logging is done using the OmniboxEditModel's records, not the
        AutocompleteInput's.
    
        There are 2 other bool keyword fields in `AutocompleteInput`:
        `prefer_keyword_` & `allow_exact_keyword_match_`; and I'll leave looking
        into whether any of these 3 can be removed in a future CL.
    
        Bug: 449785444
        Change-Id: Ib9539301edd8280117ca2e1cf4be3d1c1dfd514f
        Reviewed-on: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7797807

        tab restore behavior, since there are a lot of implementations on

commit ac2c15e6b0a83a7e3ea403e57cb8daf8a2c3625d
Author: cdesouza-chromium <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Sat May 30 00:13:55 2026 +0100

    [toolchain] Add tooling to download deps (#36860)
    
    This PR adds an experimental script to download the rust WASM toolchain
    from the bucket. This script is generic enough to be used for other
    things too (opengrep comes to mind).
    
    This download script makes use of `gclient` machinery to solve the
    condiontals for each branch. This is to mimick what one would have in a
    DEPS file. At the moment, we cannot place the download relevant data in
    the DEPS file though, and it is not clear if we ever will, but a CL has
    been submitted to `depot_tools` to start a discussion:
    https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/7881740
    
    This PR also changes how the rust WASM builder packages the toolchain,
    to match the paths where artifacts have to be deployed, so the extracing
    tooling doesn't need to know anything about it.
    
    Bug: https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/55812

commit c16b4ec7feae9b4862f11bd2882f30d71fbb911d
Author: r0hit0303 <ragarwal@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 29 18:56:20 2026 +0200

    [fingerprinting] Handle device info leaks for WebGPU  (#36817)
    
    This change scrubs the device related info from GPUAdapterInfo namely vendor, architecture and device.
    
    This change adds a patch to the upstream gpu_adapter.cc to intercept right before the moment we create the gpu adapter info, to scrub out these attributes. It was not possible to do it in gpu_adapter_info.cc as it lacked any context around ExecutionContext which was needed to get the farbling level.
    
    Below are the final behaviour with different farbling levels after this change:
    
    Farbling "off"
    - No change in behaviour i.e no scrubbing will occur.
    Farbling "balanced" with WebGLBalancedFingerprintingProtection enabled
    - Scrub the device related info from GPUAdapterInfo.
    Farbling "balanced" with WebGLBalancedFingerprintingProtection disabled
    - No change in behaviour i.e no scrubbing will occur.
    Farbling "maximum":
    - Scrub the device related info from GPUAdapterInfo. Note that this is a new behaviour and not to tied to any feature flag. For maximum farbling it makes sense to have the maximum protection.
    
    Resolves brave/brave-browser#55677

commit 0b047c271359333a5333ed7c9203d9c2ca22e9e0
Author: cdesouza-chromium <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 29 17:51:16 2026 +0100

    [toolchain] Index support for published rust WASM toolchains (#36839)
    
    This PR instroduces an index YAML file, that is both read, and updated,
    when generating rust WASM toolchain archives. The goal here is two-fold:
    
     * Provide some way for automation to be written that can query our
       bucket to see if we have any toolchain published for the given
       toolchain stem expected (OS/rust-version/clang-version/etc)
     * Prevent accidental rewrite of previously published toolchains.
    
    This is the first part of this work, as there is also the need to change
    how we sync these toolchains as well in Brave, to make sure we also make
    use of the hashsums for the toolchains, so we can detect and fail if a
    toolchain has been silently overwritten.
    
    This change also introduces the concept of a Brave subrevision. This is
    necessary for cases where we do need to regenerate the toolchain, for
    whatever good reason we may have. With the Brave sub-revision being
    added to the toolchain naming scheme, it is possible to select the new
    published toolchain as the new archive to be synced.
    
    There will be a follow-up change on how Brave is pulling these
    toolchains, but this means that with this new scheme, any rust toolchain
    update will require a commit to `brave-core` to use the new toolchain.
    This is the case in Chromium, and it should have also been the case for
    us, to guarantee the reproducibility of our builds.
    
    Bug: https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/55812

commit 1f2266520942f6d8a6f3b573b99532ada0ed7606
Author: r0hit0303 <ragarwal@brave.com>
Date:   Fri May 29 12:39:43 2026 +0200

    [query-filter] Refactor query parameter stripping logic to improve code readability (#36810)
    
    This change is a follow-up to refactor the StripQueryParameter.
    
    The refactor:
    
    a) Adds general improvements:
    
    - Improved variable names to reflect more concisely what they are capturing. For example input_kv_strings to tokens as it's not guaranteed that it will contain a key-value string all the time.
    - Rely on c++ auto bindings to get hold of param and value.
    - Replace the int disallowed_count with a bool did_strip.
    - Rely on an existing base::FindOrNull to check if an entry occurs inside a map instead of proxying via the member method count.
    - Adds comment for non-trivial filtering logic with examples.
    
    b) Replaces the use of base::SplitStringPiece to base::SplitStringOnce when splitting a single token from tokens.
    
    c) Unwinds the complicated if statement into smaller chunks to capture the flow better.
    
    Resolves brave/brave-browser#55717

commit a98075eba4c91fc189d841f9d3b9f1be2862f2f6
Author: Brian R. Bondy <netzen@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 18:30:05 2026 -0400

    Fix Brave Origin startup dialog showing generic taskbar icon on Linux (#36772)
    
    Set WM_CLASS / app_id on Brave Origin startup dialog widget
    
    Without these the Linux window manager has nothing to match the dialog
    to the Brave .desktop file with, so the taskbar falls back to a generic
    icon. Mirrors what ProfilePickerWidget does for the same reason.
    
    shell_integration_linux lives in //chrome/browser, which would create a
    dependency cycle if pulled into //brave/browser/ui/views/brave_origin
    directly. Route the lookup through the existing Delegate interface,
    implemented in the chromium_src startup_browser_creator override.
    
    Fixes https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/55614

    [Android] Surface Play in-app messages for subscription events (#36819)
    
    Calls BillingClient.showInAppMessages on app foreground so the Play
    Store can render its recovery dialog (declined payment, opt-in price
    change) on top of Brave. Gated on the user having an active VPN or Leo
    subscription, throttled to one call per real foreground session via an
    ApplicationStatus listener that resets only on HAS_STOPPED_ACTIVITIES /
    HAS_DESTROYED_ACTIVITIES — in-app navigation does not re-trigger.
    
    Resolves: https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/55735

commit 429c51348f45d7f67f66590c15933faf045b035b
Author: Alex <256235273+alekspop26@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 16:56:45 2026 -0400

    [VPN 2.0] Add GN buildflags for VPN Architectures 1.0 and 2.0 (#36787)
    
    To add a new BraveVpnService implementation based on Architecture 2.0,
    which must co-exist with Architecture 1.0 for quite a while, we need
    to split service's interface and implementation. All the external
    components will keep accessing VPN service via the BraveVpnService
    interface, but the implementation mostly goes into BraveVpnServiceImpl.
    
    This change revisits the approach how Brave VPN is enabled in GN.
    New flags are introduced: enable_brave_vpn_v1 and enable_brave_vpn_v2.
    Currently, only V1 architecture is implemented, hence, the GN flag
    enable_brave_vpn_v1 is enabled by default, and enable_brave_vpn_v2
    is disabled by default. enable_brave_vpn becomes a dependent flag:
    it is enabled when either enable_brave_vpn_v1, or enable_brave_vpn_v2,
    or both are enabled.
    
    Implements part of https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/54597

commit 6eb3287fd9f2e4dc2d3266d709edc7c76a76d097
Author: AlexeyBarabash <AlexeyBarabash@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 23:44:28 2026 +0300

    [cr149][Android][Sync] Migrate sync_everything option to per-type on Android (#36815)
    
    * [cr149][Android][Sync] Migrate sync_everything option to per-type on Android
    
    Starting from cr149 there is no `Sync Everything`
    UI option on Android.
    Android apps which had `Sync Everything` and were
    updated from cr148 to cr149 cannot modify any types,
    because of failed `DUMP_WILL_BE_CHECK(!IsSyncEverythingEnabled());`
    at `SyncUserSettingsImpl::SetSelectedType`.
    
    So this commit migrates sync_everything option to
    per-type on Android.
    
    Resolves https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/55862

commit e6ea5cd2f23d8beac6d6e246dcdff17f99291242
Author: Jocelyn Liu <yrliou@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 10:48:52 2026 -0700

    [AI Chat] Deprecate conversation API v1 (#36767)
    
    - Drop feature flag and v1 routing
    The Conversation API v2 client (OpenAI-compatible) has been the default
    since kAIChatConversationAPIV2 shipped as ENABLED_BY_DEFAULT. Always route
    Leo model engines to the v2 implementation, retire the feature flag, and
    de-parameterize the two AI Chat browser tests that toggled it.
    
    - Remove unused v1 implementation
    
    - Drop redundant V2 suffix
    
    History note: the canonical paths were previously occupied by v1 sources
    (removed in 2/3). After this rename, \`git log --follow <path>\`,
    \`git blame\`, and GitHub's history view follow the rename and surface
    the v2 development history. Plain \`git log <path>\` continues to show
    v1's history at those paths up to its removal, then the rename arriving
    from the V2-suffixed paths.

commit a7cb22bb671a4aa980dadcef1e8315feca2d472d
Author: cdesouza-chromium <cdesouza@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 14:44:40 2026 +0100

    [toolchain] A bootstrap for `depot_tools` (#36811)
    
    This bootstrap script will allows us to have a stable environment
    across all bots runnning toolchain scripts.
    
    The basics of this script is that we can chain it with the toolchain
    ones, and it takes care that we have a valid `vpython` install to run
    our tools on. It is possible to use both a url to download a script, or
    to provide a local one.
    
    This is being done to correct some of the issues we are having in CI
    with python deps, but it will also permit us to come up with subrevision
    schemes for toolchains that take into account the hashing of the
    builder.
    
    Bug: https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/55812

    [VPN 2.0] Move ClearSubscriberCredential from "browser" to "common" (#36763)
    
    To add a new BraveVpnService implementation based on Architecture 2.0,
    which must co-exist with Architecture 1.0 for quite a while, we need
    to split service's interface and implementation. All the external
    components will keep accessing VPN service via the BraveVpnService
    interface, but the implementation mostly goes into BraveVpnServiceImpl.
    
    This change moves ClearSubscriberCredential from a helper located in
    a "browser" directory, to utils located in a "common" directory. This
    function is used outside of the Brave VPN targes, so an additional
    dependency on V1's "browser" there is unnecessary.
    
    Implements part of https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/54597

commit 483a4fbd26747aaf04c86b19850f7e21ae2aefbf
Author: r0hit0303 <ragarwal@brave.com>
Date:   Thu May 28 13:40:28 2026 +0200

    [farbling] Add WebGLExtensionHandler to handle extensions related calls (#36762)
    
    This change adds a dedicated `WebGLExtensionHandler` handler to handle farbling around WebGL's `getSupportedExtensions` and `getExtension` calls. The  handler is instantiated taking into account different levels of fingerprinting protections as follows:
    
    #### 1) Balanced fingerprinting protections:
      - [WebGLBalancedFingerprintingProtection](https://sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/brave/brave-core/-/blob/chromium_src/third_party/blink/common/features.cc?L63) **enabled**:  calls to `getSupportedExtensions` will injects a fake extension to the list and will keep this new list consistent till the lifetime of that handler. Calls to getExtension on the fake extension would return a fake `ScriptObject` with the name of the fake extension in CamelCase.
      - [WebGLBalancedFingerprintingProtection](https://sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/brave/brave-core/-/blob/chromium_src/third_party/blink/common/features.cc?L63) **disabled**: No change in behaviour i.e we don't farble and return the true list of supported extensions.
    
     #### 2) Maximum fingerprinting protections:
     - No change in behaviour i.e we continue to return a single entry for the getSupportedExtensions call viz. WEBGL_debug_renderer_info.
    
     #### 3) No fingerprinting protections:
     - No change in behaviour. We return the true list of supported extensions.
    
    Please note that this is part of the change from the bigger [PR](https://github.com/brave/brave-core/pull/36605). The `WebGLExtensionHandler` would later be created by [BraveSessionCache](https://sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/brave/brave-core/-/blob/third_party/blink/renderer/core/farbling/brave_session_cache.h). This integration with `BraveSessionCache` and then with `WebGLRenderingContextBase` would be followed in later CLs.
    
    This change also adds unit_tests for the same. Browser tests would be followed up later once we have the full integration complete.
    
    <!-- Add brave-browser issue below that this PR will resolve -->
    Related https://github.com/brave/brave-browser/issues/55858
